從「不名一文」起至一販數十金止的吃客。或許會依次妒忌的。但是能夠「裝飽肚子。」總是上上了。我們想到那億萬個被災的同胞。他們的五官四肢五　六腑。難道和我們的生得不同嗎。連草根樹皮都覓不到。做一個「倒冷飯」同志。着賢没有福分哩。

戲劇

戰爭與和平　（四八）（四幕劇）

— 鶴

第四幕　往何處去？第一塲

要辦的事便是收　　　　　老百姓呢，天生來就是給他們皮　筋的。等到只剩幾根骨頭的時候，他們還要來吸我們的骨髓！老百姓和官老爺之間便是這樣的。可是我家裏的人全給砲火殺盡了，我家的草棚子也給燒得找不着方向了。只留着我一個光桿兒在義勇軍的隊伍裏，我手裏有的是槍，再看他們來向我要錢罷，我可以給他一粒子彈。　　兵甲：對了，痛快！可是還有許多多没有槍的呢？他們怎樣？他們就等着死嗎？

兵乙：那還不是一樣，不願死的到義勇軍裏面來！

兵丙：（自左急忙上）快走，快走，日本兵來清鄕了。

兵辛：有多少人？

兵丙：不知道，聽說不過是百多條槍，是這裏的村長請來的，快要進村了。　　兵甲：我們爲什麽要走呢？是隊長的命令嗎？

兵丙：那當然囉，他說我們人少，他們人多，我們犯不着損失實力。

兵辛：這說得很對，我們暫時散開一下，回頭等他們走了再說。

兵甲：不，這是什麽話？我們又不是和日本兵捉迷藏，我們爲什麽要躱開呢？我們到什麽地方去襲擊他們。　　兵乙：好的，我們到這邊村口去埋伏起來。（見排長自左上。）排長，我們還有一架機關槍，爲什麽要逃呢？這邊村口有一條小路，兩面是山，他們回去一定要走那兒過的。

兵戊：對了，那一條路我也知道得清楚，間直不必用槍，只消在兩面山上倒些大石塊下去，都可以將他們打死得乾乾凈凈。

兵丙：但是隊長的命令要我們退。

排長：那没有關係，隊長不會不准我們打日本兵的。可是你們都知道那一條　？

兵戊：知道的，我負責任好了。

排長：好的，就是你們這一小隊去。還有人呢。

兵丁：他們在那面樹林裏，我們要走那兒過的。

（他們帶着武器從台右下。）

（舞台暫時沉靜，約一分鐘，微聞急促的脚步聲。又少傾，一靑年極緊張的自左上，隠入大樹後，又少傾，有聲音自遠處傳來）

聲：大和尙……大和尙……

靑年：他嗎的，喊什麽呀！

聲……大和尙（另一靑年自左上。）

靑年：你在這裏，到底是怎麽一回事？　　靑年：我家裏現在怎樣了？

靑年乙：你妺把七公公喊去了，他在向周三爺討情。

靑年：他嗎的，總有一天，我總要將他斬成肉醬。

靑年乙：你告訴我，到底是怎麽一回事呀！

靑年：七八天以前周三爺跑到我家裏收債，你想這個時候兒誰還有錢還債呢？我說「没有」。「没有嗎？」他說：「没有就可了事嗎？」我說「你打算怎麽的？」後來他說：「和的，你等着罷，看你還不還我。」就因爲這樣，他恨極了，跑到縣城裏去告我，說我是漢奸。說我勾通日軍，勾通什麽李ＸＸ的步隊，和政府作對。你想他無恥呀。

1933.10.16

Fang Ji Surrounded on All Sides, in a Very Difficult Situation. Japanese Soldiers Launch Fierce Artillery Attacks, National Army Strictly Blocks and Intercepts. Wang Zhongfu Arrives in Beiping to Negotiate Reorganization. He Yingqin Proposes that Fang Ji First Leave the Army. Fang Ji Has No Sincere Intention to Accept the Conditions. Japanese Planes Bomb Fang's Position.

(Beiping) After Fang Ji's two units fled to the Dulinzhuang area, they were in constant contact with the Shunyi garrison. Yesterday's battle was relatively fierce. At the same time, in order to prevent Fang Ji's troops from heading east, the Japanese army used seventy military vehicles two days ago to transport Japanese soldiers from Gubeikou to the south of Niulanshan to attack Fang Ji's two units. Each vehicle carried fifteen or sixteen people, totaling about a thousand people. Yesterday, they began shelling Fang Ji's two units, and the shelling continued until night. The sound of artillery rumbled, and it could be heard clearly in Miyun and Huairou. This morning, the sound of artillery was intermittent, and it stopped slightly at noon. There was no fighting in the afternoon. Fang Ji's two units are now surrounded on all sides and are in a very difficult situation. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) He Yingqin convened a meeting of generals at Jurentang yesterday to discuss in detail the disposition of Fang Ji's remnant troops. At 11 o'clock last night, Fang sent Division Commander Wang Zhongfu and Ji's Division Commander Zhang Yangxin, and Chief of Staff Ma Yingming to Beiping to meet with military and political authorities and negotiate reorganization methods. It is said that Fang Ji still intends to request that Changping and Shunyi be designated as his defense areas. Wang, Zhang, and Ma returned to Dongxi Dulinzhuang to report. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Military dispatch: Yesterday afternoon at around 3 o'clock, in order to prevent Fang Ji's remnant troops from fleeing east, the Japanese army transferred a unit of artillery from Miyun and fired more than a hundred shells at Fang's position. At the same time, two Japanese planes dropped six or seven bombs in the Dongxi Dulinzhuang area, causing heavy damage to Fang's troops. This morning, two more Japanese planes flew to Fang's position and bombed, and the extent of the damage is unknown. Our army is currently monitoring the situation closely, fearing that they will flee elsewhere. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Fang Ji's representatives Wang Zhongfu and others passed through the defense line of General Shang Zhen and were led by Shang Zhen to Jurentang to meet with He Yingqin for a long talk. Wang and others left at 6 o'clock this morning. It is advocated here that Fang Ji must first leave the army and be conveyed to Wang and others. There has been no response as of this afternoon. It is said that Fang Ji will never accept the authorities' proposal. Sending Wang and others to Beiping this time is still a formality. Wang Zhongfu has been dismissed by Fang. It is said that he will not leave Beiping. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Shunyi telegraphs that Fang Ji's army, entrenched in Dongxi Dulinzhuang in Xiangmen Village, has no ability to escape due to the strict defense and interception by the National Army. Yesterday afternoon, from 2 to 4 o'clock, the National Army used artillery fire to threaten Xiangmen Village. Ji's soldiers were scattered in the field, and the order was very chaotic. Fang Youjun was in the army, and the general headquarters was located in the Guandi Temple in Dulinzhuang. There were more than two thousand people in Fang's unit, under Fang's personal command. A temporary grain and food supply office was set up in the village to forcibly extort money from the village chiefs and deputy chiefs of each village. If they did not pay the grain and food supply, they would pay cash. Today at around 6 o'clock, two Japanese planes flew to Fang's army's position and dropped eleven bombs, destroying several houses in Dulinzhuang. Dozens of Fang's soldiers were killed or injured, and more than twenty farmers were killed or injured. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) After Fang Ji led his troops to collapse, there were still a few remnants near Tangshan and the Ming Tombs. The National Army is currently searching and suppressing them. In the Niulanshan area, there are currently more than seven hundred Japanese troops restricting Fang Ji's remnant troops from fleeing east. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Japanese army stationed in Miyun, Shixia Town, and Gubeikou has about thirty or forty soldiers in each place. (15th Dispatch)

Li Jichun's Troops Departed Eastward from Luanzhou Yesterday

Changli: Li Jichun's troops left Luanzhou by train on the 15th and departed eastward for Beidaihe. Magistrate Liang presented Captain Fu, who was injured in the Zhanggezhuang battle, with one hundred yuan in recognition of the Security Team's courageous resistance. All sectors of Changli also raised eight hundred yuan, which was distributed to the injured and deceased police officers. The First District Defense Regiment was ordered to defend and block Lu'ankou. Yesterday morning, bandits heading to Huan were repelled by the regiment, and one hostage was rescued, and four donkeys and mules were shot down. There are no traces of bandits on the west bank of the Yanghe River. Representatives of the Funing people visited Magistrate Liang on the 15th, requesting that Liu Xingpei be transferred back east. The people plan to recover Funing. There are currently about six hundred bandits inside and outside Funing City. The bandit leaders seem to be Haijiao and Erlong. After being killed by us, the bandits are offering rewards to find their remains. (15th Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan Arrives in Beiping with Qin Dechun. Representatives from Tang and Liu Also Arrive. They Declare that They Did Not Conspire with Fang Ji.

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan arrived in Beiping tonight from Zhangjiakou with Qin Dechun, Yang Zhennan, Tian Gangyi, representative of Liu Guitang, Wu Jiabin, commander of Tang's troops, and Sun, a representative. Tomorrow morning, they will meet with He Yingqin to report on the handling of military affairs and the aftermath in Chahar Province. Song said that he came here because he received a telegram from Huang Shao-hsiung, setting the 18th as the date for a plenary meeting, so he rushed to participate. The military and political aftermath in Chahar Province has been largely handled, and local order in various counties is gradually being restored. A small number of remaining soldiers and bandits have begun to be suppressed. The rumors circulating in Beiping that Liu Jiatang and Tang Yulin's troops joined forces with Fang Ji's two units are not true. He specifically invited one or two representatives from Liu and Tang to come to Beiping to meet with He Yingqin and report on the recent situation of the two units. The matter of Prince De of Inner Mongolia convening an autonomy conference has not yielded results because there are very few adherents, so it will not become a major problem. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Qin Dechun said that the various mixed troops in Chahar Province have been completely reorganized. The remaining infantry have been handed over to Zhao Dengyu to lead, and the cavalry have been handed over to Yun Rong to lead. There are another seven or eight hundred infantrymen who will serve as road protection teams. The urgent matter remaining to be handled in Chahar Province is to suppress the bandits in the Zhangbei area. Zhao Dengyu has been appointed as the commander for bandit suppression, and Zhang Yunrong as the deputy commander. Before coming to Beiping, he specifically summoned Zhao Dengyu to Zhangjiakou and gave him instructions in person. Zhao plans to return to Zhangbei immediately and begin suppressing the bandits in various units. Tang and Liu's troops are still stationed in their original defense area in Dushikou and have not been moved. However, a unit of bandits previously reorganized by Tang's troops fled a few days ago and came south along the route taken by Fang Ji's troops, seemingly to join Fang's unit. (15th Dispatch)

Sun Dianying's Advance Team Arrives at the Border Between Ningxia and Suiyuan

(Beiping) Sun Dianying's advance team is successively departing westward from Baotou and arriving at Dengkou, at the border between Ningxia and Suiyuan. (15th Telegram)

(Beiping) Wang Baoping, Sun Dianying's representative, said that after receiving the order to depart for the Qinghai Western District for land reclamation, Ma Hongkui of Ningxia telegraphed our commander, expressing his welcome. Recently, he received another telegram from Ma, suddenly saying that he had received an order from Zhu Shaoliang, prohibiting the establishment of supply stations and the passage of troops within the territory. Our army immediately relayed the telegram to He Yingqin to report everything. He Yingqin said that after receiving our army's report, he immediately telegraphed Ma to inquire about the truth. He just received a reply from Ma saying that he had indeed received Zhu's order. He Yingqin has telegraphed Zhu again to inquire about the truth. (15th Dispatch)

Bandits Attack Salt Flats in Tanggu

(Beiping) A large number of bandits attacked the salt flats in Tanggu at around 11 o'clock on the night of the 14th. They were repelled by our cavalry. The salt fields contribute greatly to revenue. Residents of Tanggu suddenly heard gunfire and, not knowing the truth, all closed their doors and extinguished their lights. Both Chinese and Japanese troops were also on alert at the same time to prevent bandit disturbances. (15th Central News Agency Telegram)

Wang Arrives in Xunyang, Transfers to Lushan to Meet Chiang. Yin and Li Go to Beijing to Meet Wang for Instructions.

(Nanchang) Wang Jingwei arrived in Xunyang on the 14th aboard a Keishi aircraft and transferred to Lushan to meet with Chiang Kai-shek to discuss important political affairs, including Inner Mongolian autonomy, provincial and county system reforms, economic revitalization after the establishment of the Bandit Suppression and Relief Committee, and bandit suppression in North China. (15th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Tong and Li Zeyi went to Beijing, carrying a mission from Huang Shao-hsiung, to report to Wang Jingwei on the handling of North China's diplomatic issues after Huang's arrival in Beiping and the situation of Sugimura's visit to Beiping. They also requested instructions regarding Yin and Li's eastward journey. After Wang meets with Chiang in Jiangxi, a decision will be made. Yin will arrive in Beijing tonight and return to Beiping if necessary after meeting with Wang, before heading east. Li Zeyi will travel by sea from Shanghai to Dalian and then transfer to Changchun. (15th Dispatch)

(Jinan) Committee Chairman Huang telegraphed that there has been progress in negotiations with Japan and that the Bandit Suppression Army is opening up eastern Luan. (15th Dispatch)

Military Branch Issues Inspection Regulations for Garrison Troops. Ji Yiqiao and Others Depart Today.

(Beiping) He Yingqin previously appointed Ji Yiqiao as the Chief Inspector of the Jinpu Line and convened meetings of the inspection committee members for days to discuss the inspection procedures. Today, the Military Branch issued inspection regulations. Ji Yiqiao and other inspection committee members have finalized the inspection procedures and are scheduled to depart from Beiping tomorrow morning to inspect Yu Xuezhong's First Army in Tianjin first, and then head south along the Jinpu Line, transferring from Pang County to the Hejian Anci area. The inspection is expected to be completed in about twenty days. (15th Dispatch)

Feng Zhanhai's Troops Ordered to Transfer Defense to the Huairou-Zhuolu Area

(Beiping) Feng Zhanhai's troops have recently been ordered by the Military Branch to transfer their defense to the Huairou, Zhuolu, and Yanqing areas. The people of these three counties have specially sent representatives to Beiping to petition the Military Branch and telegram Chiang Kai-shek and He Yingqin, requesting that the transfer be temporarily suspended. (15th Dispatch)

Sheng Shicai Telegraphs that He is Advancing to Suppress Ma Zhongying and Personally Leading Troops to Tuban.

(Beiping) Sheng Shicai telegraphed Beiping, stating that for this campaign to suppress Ma Zhongying, all troops were drawn from the old units of the Jilin, Heilongjiang, Soviet, and Mongolian armies. After taking an oath in Xinjiang on the tenth, he personally led the troops from Xinjiang to Tuban on the eleventh to suppress Ma's rebel troops and eliminate harm for the people of Xinjiang. He expects to resolve the situation completely within two weeks. This departure was welcomed by the people of Xinjiang, and Ma Shaowu, the administrative head of Kashgar, also expressed his willingness to serve as the vanguard of Ma Zhongying's rebel troops and has now gathered old troops to await deployment. The overall situation in Xinjiang is expected to stabilize in the short term. (15th Dispatch)

Russian Planes Reconnoiter Rehe Airspace

(Beiping) A person from Rehe reported that three days ago, three Russian planes suddenly flew from Outer Mongolia to Rehe and circled over Chengde for three hours. The fuselage was silver-colored, and they flew very high. The piloting skills were extremely skilled. The Japanese garrison in Rehe used anti-aircraft guns to fire on them. After a while, the Russian planes turned north and flew away. (15th Dispatch)

Japanese Detain Korean in Guangzhou

(Hong Kong) Several Japanese people, on the 12th, drove in a Japanese consular car from Shamian to Zhuyuan, Fuyin Village, Dongshan, and forcibly detained Park Yiyi, a Korean national with Shanghai County citizenship, put him in the car, and drove him back to the Japanese consulate. The Guangzhou Municipal Government has protested to the Japanese consulate. (15th Dispatch)

Han Fuju Discusses Provincial System

(Jinan) Han Fuju said that he believes that both the provincial governor system and the committee system are good. In short, governance depends on the person. Major powers still have imperial systems, which is clear evidence of this. To revitalize the countryside, it is necessary to increase people's production and protect the export of products. If a committee is established today and a research institute is established tomorrow, it will not only not increase people's production but will increase the burden, which is absolutely unacceptable. The district chief's avoidance of native place will be completed in three phases. The militia will be transferred to the province for training in three phases. This province will never extra extort a single penny from merchants and civilians; it has no other strength. (15th Dispatch)

Zhang Xueliang Telegraphed that He Will Stay in Denmark for a Short Time

(Beiping) Zhang Xueliang recently sent a telegram to Beiping reporting that he is currently in Copenhagen, Denmark, visiting Danish industry and commerce. He plans to stay in Denmark for two weeks and then transfer to Russia. He will carefully investigate the current situation in Russia and stay in Russia for a long time. (15th Dispatch)

Huang Shaoxiong's Departure to Mongolia Undecided. He Plans to Go with Zhangjia.

(Nanjing) Huang Shaoxiong said that the departure to Mongolia is around the 20th. He is currently purchasing silk, tea, and other gifts to present to the princes and nobles of various leagues and banners when he arrives in Mongolia to express his personal intentions. The central government's outline for handling Mongolian autonomy has been discussed but still awaits formal decision by the Executive Yuan. Zhangjia is currently in Beiping and plans to accompany him to Mongolia. It is not certain where the Panchen Lama is now. After arriving in Mongolia, in addition to going to Zhangjiakou, he also plans to visit other leagues and banners if time permits. He will return to Nanjing in about a month to report. (15th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Bai Rui and other Mongolian compatriots in Beijing wrote to Prince De, asking him to pay attention to national defense and prevent the invasion of violent Japanese as the most important principles for preparing for Mongolian autonomy. (15th Dispatch)

Guihua: Shi Huayan, the General Manager of Sui Reclamation Affairs, was dispatched by telegram from Yan Xishan, and on the ninth, he visited the Panchen Lama in the Fourth Prince's residence. Because the Panchen moved to the Xialamuluo Temple, ninety miles north of the Prince's residence, on the same day to chant scriptures and spread the Dharma, Shi chased after him. He returned to Sui after the audience on the thirteenth. Shi said that according to the Panchen, the occurrence of Inner Mongolian autonomy was due to: first, the estrangement between the Mongolians and the interior; second, the influence of Outer and Eastern Mongolia; and third, the Chahar Incident. At present, most of the princes and nobles and the Mongolian people still lean toward the central government and hope that Huang and Zhao will come early to discuss together and quickly formulate a proper solution. Shi said that the Panchen returned to Jialing Temple from Xia on the fourteenth. According to reliable official news, Prince De convened two meetings at Bailing, but both were inconclusive because too few people attended. On August 20 of the lunar calendar, a meeting was hastily convened again. Prince De proposed to organize an autonomous organization at a suitable location and was nominated as the drafter of the autonomous regulations, but none of the committee members responded. In September, Fu Zuoyi sent personnel to various banners to investigate and comfort them. All the members have now returned to Suiyuan. According to the loyal intent of the Mongolian banners toward the central government, there was no one who was not pleased. In particular, the Awang of Ikh Juu League and the Fourth Prince of Govi Altai League were the most sincere. The princes and nobles all hoped that Minister Huang would go north to listen to the guidance of the central government. Members sent back to the province have brought official letters from the leaders of the various leagues, mostly stating that they did not know about the Pangjiang telegram. According to the most confidential news, the personnel from various banners who attended the meeting in the Ulanqab League temple expressed to others that they were forced to come here. After returning to their banners, they would formally declare that they did not support this matter. They requested that it be confidentially reported to Chairman Fu and conveyed to the central government to avoid being implicated in the future. Reports that the Suiyuan provincial government sent troops to the temple to suppress the Inner Mongolian conference are entirely rumors fabricated by bad people to stir up trouble and are absolutely untrue. (15th Central News Agency Telegram)

Bandits in Northern Fujian Re-Offend Lichuan and Nancheng. Bandits in the Jianning-Tai Ning Area Suffer Heavy Losses. Yongxin County Seat Will Soon Be Recovered.

(Nanchang) Good news: The main force of the bandits invaded Lichuan and Nancheng from northern Fujian. Our army bravely met the attack, killing many bandits in Xiaoshi, Xinfeng Street, and the Lichuan area. Fighting is still ongoing. (14th Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) The bandit troops of the Pseudo Fifth Army Corps have been in fierce fighting with our army in the Yuan Kou Bridge and Xinben Street area on the Jianning-Tai Ning border for several days and have suffered heavy losses. Pseudo Division Commander Xu Yangang was killed in battle. The remnant bandits have now retreated to the Lita and Tian Shi areas of Tai Ning. More than four hundred bandits of the Pseudo Eighth Division in Liancheng and Yong'an fought with our army for two hours in Jiuxian on the fourteenth. Dozens of bandits were killed and they were unable to withstand the attack and fled elsewhere. (15th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed Guangdong on the eleventh that the Ge Zhongshan Brigade of our Sixth Division conducted guerrilla warfare from Licun and went deep into Feiyan, defeating the bandit army. On the return journey to Xun Kou, they were ambushed and engaged in a fierce battle with the main force of Peng's bandits for a day and a night. They were rescued by the Sixty-ninth Division, which brought the Three Three Regiment back to Licuan. The Three Four Regiment was finally cut off at Xun Kou and fought alone for a day and a night. When their food and ammunition were exhausted, they were trapped and waited for rescue. The Fifth and Sixth Divisions organized a valiant team to rescue them and finally thwarted the enemy's attack, and the entire regiment withdrew. (15th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Wang Chen and others of the Western Route are leading the suppression campaign toward Yongxin. The county seat will soon be recovered. Commissioner Li telegraphed the county magistrate to advance with the army. (14th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The city defense commander of this city has been inspecting various defense works for days, preparing for winter defense in advance. (14th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Good news: (1) Taking advantage of the Zhu-Mao main force fleeing to Fujian, Guangdong and Hunan planned to wipe out the Pseudo Eighth Army on the west bank of the Gan River. Li Zhenqiu and Chen Zhang advanced toward Suichuan, and Wang Dongyuan advanced toward Yongxin. Both sides attacked in concert. The bandits believed that the Guangdong army was always sharp and took a defensive stance against it, attacking the Hunan army with their main force. The fighting was fierce in Getian. The bandits suffered heavy losses and retreated back to their old nest in Yongxin. Yongxin County seat will soon be recovered. (2) More than a thousand Red soldiers of the Pseudo Fifteenth Army Corps invaded Pao Ma Gang in Anyuan. Zhang Meixin and Chen's regiment retreated to lure the bandits out of the bamboo forest. The public security troops surrounded them and killed 500 bandits, seizing two repeating cannons and four machine guns. (3) Yu Hanmou has successfully eliminated scattered bandits near bandit nests in the bandit suppression area and will implement the second step of attacking the bandit nests. (4) The bandits in Licuan and Nancheng have collapsed after our bloody battles and fierce attacks. The headquarters greatly praised Zhang Yougu for detecting and bombing the Red bandits. (15th Dispatch)

Tao Guang and Li Jue's Two Divisions Concentrated in the Pingxiang-Liling Area. Xiao's Bandits Defeated, Defenses Consolidated.

(Changsha) Liu Yinggu telegraphed that Tao Guang and Li Jue's two divisions concentrated in Pingxiang and Liling, defeating the Xiao bandits who had invaded Laoguan. The Pingxiang-Liling railway and telegraph lines have been repaired, and the defenses are consolidated. The bandits who fled to the Lu Gongpi area south of Pingxiang were bombed by planes, killing many bandits. The bandits have an appearance of fleeing south. He Yingqin is still staying in the province. He Yingqin has set up a salt monopoly bureau in Pingxiang, Chaling, and Changshou Street, with Zhang Muxian as the general manager. (15th Dispatch)

He Chengjun Encountered Danger Twice on His Way to Sichuan. He Remains in Wuhan for Recuperation and Will Not Go to Jiangxi for the Time Being.

(Hankou) Chen Guangzu said that He Chengjun's entry into Sichuan invited the jealousy of reactionaries and bandits. One day at noon, dozens of miles from Chengdu, he was almost assassinated. He encountered danger again on the return journey. He is currently staying in Wuhan for recuperation due to illness and will not go to Jiangxi for the time being. The rumor that he has gone to Jiangxi is not true. (15th Dispatch)

The National Commerce is Sluggish, Customs Revenue is Affected. There Has Been Some Improvement in October.

(Nanjing) Ministry of Finance information: Since the outbreak of the Rehe War, the country's commerce has been sluggish, and customs revenue has been similarly affected. This summer's tax revenue has sharply decreased. In the four months of June, July, August, and September, monthly revenue decreased by as much as 10 million yuan compared to previous years. October is originally a peak month, and tax revenue has shown some improvement. Although detailed reports from the General Affairs Department have not been received, the increased revenue this month is estimated to be around 2 million yuan. Regarding the issue of receiving the Yuhai Customs, the personnel of the customs have already gone, and normal operations should be restored soon. (15th Dispatch)

Current Commentary

From Colonial Economy to Controlled Economy

— You

Controlled economy. This has now become an issue of national attention. We believe that under the goal of developing the national economy, what should be deeply understood is not whether economic control should be sought, but whether a controlled economy can be controlled. If this level is not recognized, the result may be drawing a tiger but resembling a dog, which is useless and harmful.

The realization of a controlled economy must have the following preconditions:

First, there must be a financially strong central hub. In general capitalist countries with extremely developed economies, there is the Bank of England in the UK, the Federal Reserve Bank in the US, and the Bank of Japan in the neighboring Japan. These central banks can exert supreme power in terms of overall foreign exchange, unified issuance, and control of credit. In our country, in addition to the Central Bank, even with the support of extremely large domestic commercial banks, it is still not enough to reduce the power of foreign banks. The power of foreign banks lies in absorbing huge amounts of deposits and controlling overall foreign exchange. Not only do they issue their own banknotes, but they can also refuse to accept our country's bank notes. In this case, if strict methods of controlled economy are to be implemented, it will inevitably be like chasing sparrows with a jungle, which is useless and harmful. Moreover, the position of these [foreign banks' power] in our country's financial market is no different from their position in India, Nanyang, and Hong Kong. They have long since gradually reduced our country to the level of a colony. In this way, how can control be effective?

Second, there must be methods to control foreign capital and commodities. In many European and American countries at present, the activities of foreign capital are mostly managed by the government and limited to a very small scope. The import and export of foreign commodities are absolutely subject to strict state supervision. These are all strict controls that they have implemented in order to save the crisis in their domestic industry and commerce. What about our country? Commodity imports exceed exports by as much as 90 million yuan annually. Foreign capital in China has exceeded one million yuan, and the annual increase in investment is no less than 200 million. If controlled economy is to seek a fundamental solution, it must first restrict the activities of foreign capital and commodities in our country's market.

The main significance of controlled economy must be to cultivate the accumulation of domestic capital and guide the upward trend of industrial and commercial profits. It cannot be achieved by chanting empty slogans or engaging in minor matters. As far as our country's current agricultural, industrial, commercial, and national economy are concerned, there is indeed a need to seek control in order to save the crisis. But if its preconditions are not paid attention to, how can a controlled economy be realized? Therefore, the center of the problem should be to first study how to break away from the current colonial economy.

Bangkok Turns into a Battlefield. The Government is Confident it Can Control the Overall Situation.

Bangkok - Government forces defending Bangkok are bombarding with artillery.

The rebellious crowd led by Prince Bovaradej, the former Prince of the Revolution, cannot advance. Fierce fighting is still in progress. The sound of artillery can be heard here, but details of the war are unknown due to strict inspection. Two reconnaissance planes on the side of the revolutionary army flew over Bangkok yesterday. One plane was shot down into the river. The government has repeatedly stated that it is definitely able to control the overall situation, so the public is a little more at ease today. Residents in the suburbs were warned by the authorities and are now flocking to the city for refuge. (15th Reuters Telegram)

Discovery of Anti-Manchu Officials

(Harbin) The authorities recently arrested a Manchu official of the Chinese Eastern Railway after discovering a conspiracy to overthrow the [Manchu] government. The person's surname and name have not yet been released, but it is said that he is the chief of a certain section. His office was searched, and various documents of conspiracy were found. The head of the Japanese Special Police announced this matter today, saying that detectives are still investigating thoroughly and hope to arrest several people behind the scenes within days. (15th Reuters Telegram)

Germany's Disconnection with the League of Nations, Armed Nations Take it as an Ally, Strengthen the Belief in Expanding Military Strength. British Prime Minister Grasps the Key to Salvaging the European Situation. Difficulties in the Disarmament Issue. New Ways Will Be Found to Solve It. The General Committee is Scheduled to Meet Today.

(Tokyo) This time, Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations served as an opportunity to cooperate with Japan, which has the same position. It is also a matter of concern whether Japan's shipbuilding movement will stimulate it. Europe, especially London, is very worried. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs is handling this matter with extreme calmness. The following is a record of its views: (1) Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations this time is to break away from the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles as a defeated country and seek a way out to establish its national equality. This is a natural and foreseeable move. Japan has no sense of surprise. (2) Japan only seeks to thoroughly exercise its foreign policy. It is not necessary to participate in the liquidation of European changes. Europe is Europe, Asia is Asia. The national opinion has completely agreed to decide its own policy based on this individual concept. (3) In view of this national opinion, Europeans believe that Japan will cooperate with Germany or have some attempt, holding a dangerous view. This is ironclad evidence that European countries still lack an understanding of the Far East and is also the reason why Germany withdrew from the League of Nations. (4) The discussion that Japan will launch a shipbuilding movement can also be said to be a prelude to German-Japanese cooperation. However, Japan's shipbuilding is within the quality and quantity allowed by the London Treaty, so this situation is nothing more than a solitary worry. (15th Japanese United News Telegram)

Japanese Militarists Sympathetic to Germany

(Tokyo) Regarding Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations, the Japanese naval authorities view it with unusual gravity. Their opinions are as follows: Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference is a very significant issue. It will be especially difficult to resolve the disarmament conference in the future. Even British Prime Minister MacDonald said that if the disarmament conference fails to be resolved, Europe will fall into chaos. This shows that this is not just a major problem for Europe, but a major problem for the world. (15th, Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) After the occurrence of Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference, the Japanese army authorities' speculation is as follows: After the great excitement of the European war, and then being bound by the Treaty of Paris, the national sentiment of Germany has been strengthened. At the disarmament conference, they requested equality of armaments with England, France, and Italy, which is something that deserves sympathy. However, the country actually carried out the withdrawal from the disarmament conference. It can be seen that they have no regard for Germany and cannot reduce their armaments, so it is natural that they will fall apart. The reason is very clear. However, regarding this case, what Hitler's decision will be and what his attitude will be in the future are the most interesting questions. From now on, the nationalism of various countries will become increasingly stronger, and the powers will become opposing not only in terms of armaments, but also economically. (15th, Japan United Press)

Diplomatic Strategy to Undergo Changes

Diplomacy and international influence are very significant. Therefore, Prime Minister Saito ordered Foreign Minister Hirota to investigate the truth. Foreign Minister Hirota will report on the details at tomorrow's five-minister conference. At the same time, he will also express the empire's determination regarding future diplomatic policies. Furthermore, Minister of the Army Araki and Minister of the Navy Osumi believe that if the League of Nations and the disarmament conference become nominal, the countries of Europe and the United States may shift towards nationalism, and establishing national policies in Japan will be even more important. Therefore, the five-minister conference is more noteworthy than before. (15th, Den Tsushin)

Hitler's Broadcast Speech Condemns Victorious Nations: Countries Use Oppression as Their Skill; Peace is Based on Sincere Cooperation

(Berlin) German Chancellor Hitler made a broadcast speech here tonight, which was broadcast nationwide by various German radio stations, stating that if France and Germany can eliminate violence from their common lives, it will be a great undertaking for all mankind.

Obey the Peace Treaty, Sheathe Our Swords

Hitler recalled the events since the armistice in 1918, saying that at that time, Germany trusted President Wilson's Fourteen Points, so it sheathed its swords. If the world had extended its hand to the broken country in a fair manner in the years after the armistice, mankind could have saved countless hardships. Germany has exhausted its efforts to heal the wounds of its enemies. When Germany obeyed the peace treaty and destroyed weapons in order to facilitate world disarmament, all the people of the world thought that this was the starting point of common-sense victory.

Victorious Nations' Arrogant Attitude is Oppressive

Germany has the right to hope that the rest of the world will fulfill its promises, but unfortunately, the political leaders of other countries are all arrogant people with the air of victors. They do not know that the recovery of the world depends on the sincere cooperation of all countries and the elimination of the psychology of war, not on the slave labor of the ravaged countries. All the belligerent countries are confident that they have not committed the crime of willingly being the leader of the army. Since they have this confidence, they should not have permanent enmity and deliberately retain the memory of the catastrophe.

No War Fantasies Against France

Although the German people demand the rights promised by the peace treaty, Germany has no territorial disputes other than the disputes between France and Germany. When the Saar region is returned to Germany, anyone with a clear understanding will not have the illusion that war can break out between France and Germany. German youth do not engage in demonstrations against France, but only focus on the political movements necessary to curb communism. If all countries in the world build indestructible fortresses, build huge aircraft, heavy artillery, and tanks for their own purposes, then one cannot accuse the National Socialist Party, which marches in unarmed formations, of being a great harm to the world.

Not Willing to Live in an Inferior Position

Other countries all have the right to self-defense, but Germany alone does not. This is simply treating the German people as a lower class. The people currently in power in Germany are completely different from the bribed traitors of November 1918. We are not responsible for the war, nor are we responsible for the events that occurred in the war, but we are responsible for doing something for our suffering people, as anyone with a sense of honor must do. (14th, Reuters)

Slander Against Germany Intensifies

(Berlin) Hitler said in his speech that various countries have slandered Germany in various ways, such as the ridiculous drama of holding an investigation in London regarding the [German Reichstag fire case]. This is something that Germany cannot tolerate. He also said, [The French government under the leadership of the current Prime Minister says that there is no intention to threaten or insult the German nation. We are deeply moved by this and have hope for the future. We respectfully listen to this statement].

Military Equality is All We Seek

He then said that Germany does not demand rearmament; what it seeks is only equality of rights. Therefore, if the international community recognizes that certain countries can set up certain weapons, then, based on the principle of equality, Germany can also set them up. If this is denied, it is actually treating Germany as a second-class country, which Germany cannot accept. Germany joined the League of Nations and the disarmament conference originally hoping that the German nation would enjoy equal rights with other nations. If this cannot be done, it is actually inflicting an unbearable insult on Germany. When Hitler made this statement, his voice was extremely high. He went on to say that all countries have made promises to reduce armaments, and Germany has fulfilled its obligations to the extreme. At this time, other countries with powerful armaments should fulfill their promises. Hitler also said that the German race requires no threat to other countries. What Germany demands is not the establishment of offensive weapons, but the establishment of defensive weapons that all countries can possess and are not prohibited by future disarmament.

Sincere Cooperation, Hope for Peace

Hitler concluded, [We are representatives of an honest nation and are ourselves people who cherish honor. Therefore, we cannot participate in certain constructions that only people who disregard honor can tolerate. It is only beneficial to negotiate with people who cherish honor in the international community. Why associate with unreliable people and enter into treaties with them? All countries in the world should consider the sense of honor of such governments. Only in this kind of atmosphere can a method of building peace be carried out.

Congressional Re-election to Gauge Public Opinion

The current German government has dissolved the House of Representatives and is holding re-elections to gauge German public opinion. All countries in the world should know that the German government's love of peace and its concern for honor can represent the same psychology of the German people. He also said that this move is to allow the people to express their faith and will have significant value in history. The government is making the people vote not only to make them approve of the principles adopted by the government, but also to make them deeply believe in these principles and become one with them.

Vow to Fight for Equality and Honor

Hitler concluded, [All countries in the world, seeing this kind of expression, must deeply believe that the German government and the people are united in the struggle for equality and honor. The German government and the people have only one hope: to help the world end the era of painful mistakes and regrettable hatred, and that the people of Europe, who are least related to world civilization, will all be reconciled]. Hitler's speech was broadcast at one o'clock in the morning (local time) and was translated into English, French, Spanish, and Portuguese for broadcast abroad. (14th, Havas)

The Door to Negotiations on the Disarmament Issue is Not Closed: Seeking a Clever Way to Break the Deadlock; France Suggests Inviting the British Prime Minister to be a Peacemaker

Rome: It was announced this afternoon that [The situation has reached this point and should be examined in its current state, and possible methods should be studied to reach a compromise]. It also stated that Prime Minister Hitler's tone did not block the door to negotiations, but [Since Germany has withdrawn from the disarmament conference, the disarmament conference cannot continue to be held. It is bound to be postponed until the necessary and sufficient conditions are realized before the overall problem is fully discussed anew]. (15th, Havas)

(London) Germany's sudden withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference was completely unexpected. The reactions of politicians from various countries have caused a common feeling in diplomatic circles here that the situation cannot be taken lightly. A very clever way must be found to allow the countries to reach a common understanding, and then the issue of the Saar can be thoroughly discussed. After carefully examining the opinions within the capitals of major countries, many politicians are looking to Britain to provide the key to the solution. The French side has especially informally suggested that British Prime Minister MacDonald be invited to be a peacemaker again. In addition, several informal suggestions have been put forward in diplomatic circles, and British officials are seriously considering them. Some diplomats believe that Britain, Germany, France, Italy, and the United States will therefore increase the opportunity to draft a disarmament convention. In the future, Germany may be invited to participate again. Opinions from all sides seem to indicate that this matter has gone beyond the issue of armaments and that the entire post-war peace structure must be inspected and slightly modified in several aspects. It is expected that the first step will be a frank and thorough discussion with Germany, led by Britain. Regarding this matter, the German Foreign Ministry has notified the British ambassador and entrusted him to forward it to London, and also notified the chairman of the disarmament conference, Henderson. Henderson also said that he had received a letter stating that he would submit it to the General Committee on Disarmament. It is expected that if Britain takes the lead, its progress will be calm and based on completely accurate information. (15th, Kokumin)

Six-Nation Representatives Draft a Reply to Germany: Disarmament Conference Likely to be Postponed

(Geneva) The disarmament representatives of the six countries met this morning for two hours and will meet again at 5:00 p.m. to draft a reply to the note from Germany to the chairman of the disarmament conference, Henderson. Germany's letter pointed out that armed countries are unwilling to fulfill their disarmament guarantees. (15th, Kokumin)

(Geneva) The representatives of the major countries gathered this morning at the residence of the chairman of the disarmament conference, Henderson, to discuss whether the disarmament conference should continue to be held after Monday. Among the participants were British Foreign Secretary Simon, US Ambassador Davis, Italian representative Scogna, Czech Foreign Minister Beneš, and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol. (15th, Kokumin)

(Geneva) Since Germany's withdrawal from the disarmament conference and the League of Nations, the fate of the disarmament conference is currently unknown. Some delegations, especially the British delegation, advocate that the meeting must be postponed. As for the US delegation, it advocates continuing to work, as does the French delegation, but it is not as resolute as the US delegation. It is generally believed that the General Committee on Disarmament will still meet on Monday as originally scheduled. The agenda of the General Committee will roughly remain the same, that is, British Prime Minister Simon will first make a statement (he notified the Presidium yesterday), and then US representative Davis will restate the various principles approved by the Presidium yesterday. However, whether the General Committee will continue to work after that or will be postponed will only be determined when Chairman Henderson meets with the representatives of France, Britain, and Italy, as well as the rapporteur of the General Committee, Beyens. This meeting is scheduled to be held at 11:00 a.m. today, and the situation caused by Germany's actions will be studied in all aspects at the meeting. It is generally expected that the following procedure will be agreed upon: the General Committee will first listen to the report of British Foreign Secretary Simon, and then all delegations will exchange opinions and propose a motion containing the various principles already passed by the Presidium. The representatives will vote on the motion, and then the General Committee will be postponed, and the task of drafting the disarmament convention will be handed over to a drafting committee. This convention will only be implemented after Germany resumes international cooperation. (15th, Havas)

Davis Reads a Document Opposing German Rearmament

(Washington) US Representative Davis read a document from the US government at the non-public disarmament conference in Geneva today. The State Department explained that the United States, in agreement with the Allied Powers in the Great War, opposes Germany's rearmament and supports the disarmament plan that has now caused Germany to withdraw from Geneva. (15th, Reuters)

Geneva Hears a Bolt From the Blue

(Geneva) The German government's decision not to participate in the disarmament conference and to withdraw from the League of Nations was delivered to the League of Nations approximately one hour after the Presidium of the disarmament conference met. The news caused a great shock to public opinion, as people generally expected that the Berlin government would not show such surprising resistance and dissatisfaction beforehand. The disappointment and anger of the American people were no less than those of others, and they said that this morning, the German representatives in Geneva still asked the American representatives to find a way to prevent the speeches that US representative Davis and British representative Simon were about to deliver from being too firm, so as not to cause a stalemate. The reason why the British and American representatives used a cooperative tone to speak for Germany was because of this. Unexpectedly, out of the blue, Germany suddenly announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference, cutting off its own retreat. This was truly unexpected. It should be noted that Germany joined the League of Nations in September 1926 (that is, after the Treaty of Locarno was signed). This withdrawal from the League of Nations happened to be after Japan withdrew from the League of Nations. The League of Nations has suffered this serious blow, and the progress of all its affairs will encounter obstacles. As for the disarmament conference, it is now in an extremely dangerous position. However, the situation is very clear. Germany's participation in the disarmament conference was originally very reluctant. Its dealings with various countries on the green carpet were only to achieve its political goals, not to cooperate internationally. If the goal is not achieved, it will leave in a huff. Looking at it now, it is extremely obvious. (14th, Havas)

Paris Believes the Situation is Serious

(Paris) Tonight, French officials admitted that the news of Germany's notification of its withdrawal from the disarmament conference and the League of Nations came as a complete surprise.

Page 6

Those willing to comment on this matter mostly say that it is undeniable that this is the worst situation encountered by the League of Nations since the European War. Many French newspapers expect that countries will immediately begin an arms race, but some also believe that there is still hope of establishing an agreement with Germany, and advocate inviting British Prime Minister MacDonald to mediate and convene a new conference of the great powers to maintain peace. (14th, Kokuminsha)

American Mediation Becomes a Soap Bubble

(Washington) The US government feels that Germany's withdrawal from the disarmament conference is actually equivalent to the failure of two years of efforts to negotiate a disarmament agreement. Secretary of State Hull deeply regrets this action by the Germans, saying that the United States has tried its best to cooperate with the countries attending Geneva in order to cultivate a spirit of friendship and peace and avoid the occurrence of such events today. The United States had hoped that countries would continue discussions to reach a solution. Germany's actions not only hinder the entire disarmament movement, but may even bring it to a halt. It was also learned from other sources that although the United States supports Britain and France's opposition to Germany's immediate rearmament, it has also worked hard to seek understanding regarding the right to equal armaments within the security system in the future. (14th, Kokumin)

British Political Circles Adopt a Calm Attitude

(London) British Prime Minister MacDonald is currently resting at his country villa, but he is fully aware of the current situation and will return to his residence tonight. The British cabinet will probably have a formal discussion on the disarmament difficulties on Monday. British officials still maintain a calm attitude towards the disarmament difficulties. (15th, Reuters)

Mussolini Remains Silent

Rome: Italian Prime Minister Mussolini remains silent on this matter, but other key members openly admit that they do not know what to do. They say that it is difficult to comment since Germany ultimately did not violate the Four-Power Pact. (15th, Reuters)

Rome: Italian officials today denied the claim that Italy will follow Germany in withdrawing from disarmament and the League of Nations, saying that it was fabricated by Paris and has no basis, and is inconsistent with Mussolini's aim of cooperating with other countries for peace. (15th, Kokumin)

German Delegation Leaves for Home

(Geneva) After Germany announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference, the German delegation to the disarmament conference left Geneva tonight. Before leaving, even the reporters dispatched by the German press to Geneva with the German delegation were unwilling to meet. The German delegation claimed that it no longer had the right to express Germany's opinions, so meeting with the press was of no use. (14th, Havas)

Preparations Made Long Ago for Withdrawal from the League of Nations

(Berlin) The decision of Germany to withdraw from the League of Nations disarmament conference has been prepared for several days, which can be seen from the speed of the German government's actions. The German government's announcement of the declaration was already swift, and at the same time, it promulgated laws to fundamentally revise the constitutional order. This kind of internal reorganization is of utmost importance, and everyone can see it. Recently, although the German government has made extreme efforts to intensify propaganda, the situation of the German people has not improved much, and the German people cannot help but be disappointed. In order to shift the focus, Chancellor Hitler took the surprising action of withdrawing from the League of Nations, which boosted the morale of the people. Hitler's holding of a referendum after withdrawing from the League of Nations shows that his purpose is to increase his prestige domestically. The German government also wants to take the opportunity to expand the central concentration of power, completely place the German government under the dictatorship of the Nazi Party, and completely change the nature of the German state. As for diplomatic issues, Hitler must have no intention of breaking off relations. This can be seen from the speech made by Hitler. He saw that the situation in Geneva was unfavorable to Germany, so he took the opportunity to withdraw. People here believe that after Germany withdraws from the disarmament conference, the Four-Power Treaty can still be used as a remedy, so there is no need to worry about being unable to do anything. The Fourth Power Treaty is based on the League of Nations Covenant. Germany has actually neglected it and announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations, so the Fourth Power Treaty is also unable to be cited. This is something that Hitler has not seen. (15th, Havas)

Takes Effect Two Years Later

(London) Germany's resolution to withdraw from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference caused panic among the general public, who rushed to newspaper vendors to buy special editions containing the news. The general public was shocked by this news, but those who pay attention to politics had already anticipated that it might take this action, given Germany's unwillingness to make any concessions in Geneva yesterday. Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations cannot take effect within two years, but it will be like Japan, no longer sending representatives to participate in any meetings of the League of Nations. (14th, Reuters)

(Berlin) Reliable sources claimed today that the German government's intention to withdraw from the International League and the disarmament conference is to actually withdraw, but everything should be done as smoothly as possible. It also stated that Germany will still adhere to all regulations during the two-year transition period, such as paying membership fees. (15th, Kokumin)

Congressional Re-election is an Internal Tactic

(Berlin) After the German cabinet learned of the content of British Foreign Secretary Simon's speech in Geneva, it made this major decision. After the cabinet decided to withdraw from the League of Nations, German Chancellor Hitler immediately went to see President Hindenburg. The German president ultimately agreed to this decision. Hitler's resolution to appeal to the people is a tactic that allows Hitler to obtain the support of an absolute majority of the people. This is merely asking voters whether they are willing to elect National Socialist Party candidates. In fact, people outside the party are not allowed to be elected. (14th, Reuters)

French Government's Position Shaken

(Paris) The French government's position may be affected by Germany's resolution, because the financial plan established by the Ministry of the Interior this morning has no chance of passing. If so, Prime Minister Daladier will resign. Germany's action will allow the French opposition party, which does not approve of Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour's disarmament policy, to have new weapons to attack the government. The French government recognizes that the situation is serious, but its attitude is still calm. They do not know whether Germany is merely making grand statements to seek concessions, or whether it is actually closing the doors to peace and reconciliation. (14th, Reuters)

Austria Increases Border Defenses

Innsbruck: Because of new disputes with the Germans regarding the activities of the National Socialist Party, Austria views Germany's withdrawal from the disarmament conference and the League of Nations as more serious than other European countries. As soon as Vienna received the news from Berlin, it immediately ordered an increase in defenses on the German-Austrian border, apparently because Austrian officials are deeply concerned about conflicts occurring on the border. At present, barbed wire has been newly installed in many key locations, and the National Guard patrols the main roads along the border. Soldiers have also been dispatched to guard the mountain paths and trails that have never been defended before. Travelers crossing the border are strictly inspected, sometimes forced to undress and searched for secret documents. All cars are inspected by mechanics, and empty tires are often disassembled to check for smuggling. (15th, Kokumin)

Public Opinion in Various Countries

(Paris) Public opinion around the world continues to comment on the events that occurred in Berlin and Geneva yesterday, all indicating an uneasy picture of world politics. The conclusions drawn from this are extremely inconsistent. However, one point is completely agreed upon by newspapers around the world, namely, that Germany is in complete isolation in international organizations. Although German newspapers have not clearly pointed this out, they also acknowledge it. The comments of various newspapers are summarized below.

England

British newspapers raise a question: What attitude should the world adopt towards Germany? The Times advocates signing a disarmament convention to further isolate Germany and, if necessary, resorting to political, economic, and financial sanctions. If Germany continues to expand its armaments (we believe this is inevitable), then short of using force, it is futile for us to force the National Socialist Party government to abandon its established procedures.

France

[Le Temps] comments on Germany's attitude towards the League of Nations and the disarmament conference, saying, [For fourteen years, people from all countries have worked tirelessly and with great difficulty to build lasting peace between nations, but the result of their efforts has been swept away by Germany. Germany cannot but bear its responsibility to all of humanity. However, what good is this to Germany? Germany wants to obstruct the conclusion of the disarmament convention, but it must be known that even if the disarmament convention does not succeed, there is still the Treaty of Versailles, and the signatory countries will never allow the provisions of the treaty to be destroyed. Do the people in Berlin know this? Moreover, British Privy Councilor Baldwin's speech to the Birmingham Conservative Party Congress clearly warned Germany. Have the people in Berlin never understood this? Recently, the faith of people around the world in peace-building has been increasing day by day, and their desire for international harmony is strong. Suddenly seeing Germany's actions today, how can they not be filled with grief and anger and think of resisting? The disarmament conference has been frustrated by Germany and has failed, so an arms race will follow, and the danger to humanity will reach its peak, and Germany's harm to the world will be revealed. Only by having people with sincerity work together to seek self-defense can Germany's harm be eliminated. With the international situation changing to this point, I know that the nations of the world will not be able to forgive the German authorities.

America

New York seems to view the current situation as more serious than other countries. Some newspapers even believe that armed conflict is possible. What they are most concerned about is what attitude the U.S. government will take towards the various problems in Europe. The *New York Times* and the *New York Evening Post* both say that the U.S. government has decided to do everything in its power to save the disarmament conference. The *New York Times* also said that regardless of whether Germany's rearmament is true or not, the U.S. has already stood on the side of the Allied countries in the last war. Other newspapers advocate adopting a neutral attitude, but there are different opinions on what form this neutrality should take. Officials in Washington claim that the U.S. can choose between strictly adhering to neutrality and passive assistance. The so-called "passive assistance policy" has been explained by President Roosevelt as meaning that neutral countries have the right to normal exchanges with belligerent countries during wartime, which has been generally recognized by the world. The U.S. may abandon these rights. In addition, Washington believes that the German parliamentary re-election will not help the current political situation. The *New York Evening Post* said that the election was a "pathetic farce."

Italy

Italian newspapers do not express a clear attitude towards the stance taken by Germany. For example, *Il Popolo d'Italia* said that although Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference is a kind of advancement of the political situation, there is no need to be overly alarmed or fearful. Moreover, such a situation is not without a way out, and the most difficult problems can be solved outside the League of Nations and the disarmament conference. As for the German government's dissolution of the parliament, its benefits are difficult to understand. Other newspapers have similar views. Only *Il Messaggero* has a unique view, saying that Premier Hitler made a solemn guarantee of peace yesterday, which must be paid attention to. (Havas, 15th)

Austria

Austrian newspapers are unfavorable to German newspapers. They express doubt about the pacifism advocated by Hitler, saying that the German government has been continuously implementing "deceptive policies" towards Austria and cannot be trusted. They also said that this move by Germany is a big mistake, even from the perspective of its own interests. *Neues Wiener Journal* said that since Germany has withdrawn from Geneva, it should be bound by the Treaty of Versailles. *Bundespost* said that "after Germany withdrew from the disarmament conference, other countries are more free." What benefit is there for Germany to isolate itself?

Poland

The government newspaper *Gazeta Polska* stated, "Germany slammed the table, causing the Four-Power Pact to suffer a deadly wound." The French Parliament may not approve this treaty under the current circumstances. (Havas, 15th)

Switzerland

The League of Nations' newspaper *Journal de Genève* responded to the claims made by German newspapers that they hoped to conduct negotiations within the scope of the Four-Power Pact, saying that the Four-Power Pact can only be used within the scope of the League of Nations. Now that Germany has withdrawn from the League of Nations, the Four-Power Pact has died yesterday. *La Tribune de Genève* said, "This sudden event may make the relationship between Britain, France, and the United States closer." In addition, all newspapers said that although the situation is serious, it is clearer than before.

Germany

(Berlin) German newspapers do not engage in empty talk about the seriousness of the overall situation, but only say that the door is not completely closed yet. The *Berliner Tageblatt* said that Hitler's speech was moderate in tone, so it was very powerful. The *Kreuzzeitung* said that the German people are now of one mind and stand behind the President and the Prime Minister. The *Deutsche Tageszeitung* said that Hitler's speech was the voice of the German people. The *Vossische Zeitung* said that the best part of Hitler's speech was praising French Prime Minister Daladier for his noble idea of fairness, and tens of millions of Germans are very grateful for the remarks made by Daladier in his recent speeches. In short, German newspapers are not as pessimistic as foreign newspapers and hope that Hitler's solemn and pragmatic speech can close the path to final understanding. (National Telegram, 15th)

Tensions Between Japan and Russia, Washington Closely Watching, U.S. Press Advocates Joint British Action to Restrain Japan

(Washington) The State Department issued a statement due to the increasing tension between Japan and Russia, saying that the U.S. government is only watching. In addition, some people believe that winter is approaching, and Siberia and Manchuria are terribly cold, so if Japan and Russia can avoid conflict within the next four weeks, the chance of their breakup will be greatly reduced. (Havas, 14th)

(New York) The *Sunday Times* reported that European wars are about to happen again. France and Germany still need to go through centuries of conflict. The recurrence of the European war is just another scene in the conflict. "This matter has nothing to do with the United States, and it is not convenient to interfere again, because the United States has the threat of fighting Japan and must prepare for it, and it is especially not appropriate to interfere again. What the United States should do is to conclude an alliance with Britain to prevent Japan and help Australia. When Japan attacks the United States, Britain must at least use its navy to help the United States." (Havas, 14th) (London) The *Observer* said today that disturbances in the Far East have revealed the conflict between Russia and Japan. The dispute over the price of the Chinese Eastern Railway is one of them, but it is not the total cause of the conflict between the two sides. The fact that the rights of the League of Nations do not extend to Russia and Japan is also not important, because Western Europe, where the rights of the League of Nations can extend, is also in a bad state. The newspaper also said that it is no coincidence that Moscow is now trying to be friendly with Poland and France. (Reuters, 15th)

Britain Expresses Military Expansion

(London) It was expressed here today that Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference will stimulate Britain's newly rising Conservative Party to increase national defense preparations. Australia and New Zealand have decided to expand naval and air defense. Sheffield steel armor manufacturers are expecting new shipbuilding contracts, and Hoover and other arsenals are also hiring workers. (Reuters, 15th)

Japan Trains Student Soldiers as Basic Units for Scientific Warfare, Estimated at Over 734,000 People

(Tokyo) The Japanese military regards 1935 as the period for foreign wars and is preparing its military, diplomatic, economic, financial, and social countermeasures. It is reported that it has recently paid special attention to weaving student soldiers. The recruitment section of the Army Ministry (responsible for matters related to recruitment offices) has formulated new guidelines to reform the military training methods of various schools. For 1,418 universities and specialized schools across the country, with 734,602 students, strict actual combat training will be carried out. The outline of the guidelines is as follows: (1) Based on battlefield experience, student soldiers are brave in combat and extremely agile in action, and can be compared with active-duty troops. The focus should be on intensifying training with the goal of making them the basic units for the next war. (2) The training methods should focus on small-unit operations, and large-group operations must be added in the future. (3) Train for actual combat, especially focusing on scientific warfare. Student soldiers have high knowledge and are most suitable for the latest scientific warfare. (4) In order to prevent shaking of military morale, in addition to military training, special attention must be paid to ideological education. Therefore, students must have a considerable understanding of national defense, diplomacy, society, and finance based on national policies, so that they can automatically fight for patriotism. (5) Increase special training fees starting from next year. (China United Press, 15th)

India-Japan Trade Negotiations Moved from Simla to Delhi

Simla The Japan-India negotiations in Simla were temporarily suspended after the meeting on the 17th. The meetings will be held in Delhi thereafter. The Japanese delegation will take the train to Delhi from Simla on the 19th and 20th respectively. (Domei News Agency, 14th)

Sun Tonggang Arrives in Taiyuan

(Taiyuan) Sun Tonggang and Wang Zuwen took off from Shijiazhuang at 9:00 AM on the 15th and arrived in Taiyuan at 10:30 AM. The whole city flew flags, and all agencies and groups went to the airport to welcome them. Yin Tong Will Go to Changchun,奉 Huang Fu Orders Negotiation of Various Issues, Li Zeyi Invites Ariyoshi to Go North

Beiping Correspondence, After Huang Fu, Chairman of the Political Affairs Readjustment Committee, returned to the North, KITA Seichi, the representative of the Japanese Kwantung Army, arrived in Beiping. Huang had several discussions with him on Sino-Japanese issues in North China. However, due to the limited authority of Kita's representation, only some actual matters were briefly discussed, and no decision could be made. Kita has returned to Changchun to report, and although there have been telegrams back and forth, it is still not clear. Huang Fu felt that the various issues were complicated and intricate, and branch negotiations were not easy to break the current difficult situation. Therefore, on the one hand, Yin Tong was sent to Changchun to have an overall contact with the commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army, Hishikari, on various issues. If necessary, he may go to Tokyo. On the other hand, Li Zeyi was sent to Shanghai to urge the Japanese envoy Ariyoshi to go north to discuss everything in detail. Yin and Li left Beiping for Tianjin on the 12th to meet with the commander of the Japanese army, Nakamura, to exchange views. Li then took the Beiping-Pukou train south from Tianjin at 11:00 AM this morning (14th). Yin also left Tianjin for Shanhaiguan this evening (14th) and transferred to Changchun. It is said that he will go to Beiping first, but it is not yet known which is true. It is reported that OKAMURA Yasuji, Deputy Chief of Staff of the Japanese Kwantung Army, will also arrive in Beiping recently. As for the bandits in Luandong, they are becoming more active. The newly formed security team cannot go east to suppress them. It is said that they are waiting for negotiations from all parties before setting a departure date. Our side, in view of the source of the bandits often coming from outside the pass, plans to first guard all the small passes of the Great Wall to cut off the source of the bandits, and then suppress them severely, in order to eliminate them. (October 14)

A Gang of Bandits in Luandong Plans to Invade Changli, A Military Officer from a Certain Country is Arranging it, Changli Traitors are Actually Trying to Lead the Bandits into the City, Li Jichun Sends a Team to Fanning to Suppress the Bandits

Changli Correspondence, The bandit atmosphere in Luandong is becoming increasingly intense. The following is a summary of the recent situation in Luandong, as reported in yesterday's correspondence. The bandits' plan to flee to Changli is even more urgent than their plan to flee to Fanning, because Changli is the richest county in Luandong and has always been coveted by bandits. Therefore, after the bandits fled to Fanning, they planned to advance westward. The attack on the Northeast Lianggezhuang by the bandits on the 7th of this month was more intense than the battle in Fanning. In this battle, the bandits mobilized their elite troops and tried to make a desperate gamble. However, the security team arrived quickly, which was unexpected by the bandits. More than 200 bandits were killed. Bandit leaders Da Long, Er Long, and Si Haijiao were killed at the same time. After suffering this setback, the bandits became more eager to flee to Changli out of anger. They reorganized their forces and obtained the assistance of a military advisor from a certain country. It is reported that the bandits, in view of the previous failure, listened to the command of the military advisor from a certain country and formulated three plans to attack Changli: (1) Use sailboats to transport a large number of plainclothes bandits, lurking along the coast of Leting, and then transfer to Changli to disturb the rear of the security team; (2) Use money to lure our local self-defense groups to divide our strength and reduce some of our powerful enemies. The first team of the Fanning Defense Regiment, which mutinied earlier, was also bought by the bandits at a price of 20 yuan per person; (3) The bandits were originally a mob. Once on the front line, they would flee in fear. Now they have changed the strategy of attacking in echelons, with elite bandits equipped with broadswords and pistols venturing into the attack. From the above three strategies, the background of the bandits is even clearer. It is reported that Dou Xizhe, the commander of the security team, after learning of the bandits' plan, immediately changed the defense line to resist. However, the current situation in Changli is indeed surrounded by dangers. Although the people's hearts are slightly stable, the danger has not diminished.

Traitors in Changli have been carrying out activities recently. A group of traitorous merchants secretly sent representatives to Qinhuangdao to request Japanese troops to come in to seek temporary peace, and also sent representatives to Qinhuangdao to meet with bandit leader Qi Wenping, saying that the people of Changli welcomed them to enter, but because the security team was stationed in Changli, they dared not openly express their welcome. They also claimed that they had repeatedly wanted to take on the responsibility of providing relief, but were obstructed by the security team. It is reported that a certain Liu, the representative of the traitorous merchants, is still in Qinhuangdao, making various negotiations with Qi Wenping and others. There are two reasons why the traitorous merchants are so unscrupulous: one is to recognize the bandits as their fathers in order to satisfy their own official desires, and the other is to think of using the power of the bandits to protect the safety of their private property. As for the country and the people, they know nothing about it. Recently, they have prepared 10,000 yuan and will take the opportunity to pay tribute to the bandit army. On the 10th of this month, Yamatani, the captain of the Japanese gendarmerie in Qinhuangdao, and Endo, the staff officer of the Suzuki Division, visited Dou Xizhe in Changli as a private visit, and then went to the county government to visit County Magistrate Liang, asking County Magistrate Liang to raise some supplies for the bandits locally. County Magistrate Liang immediately refused. The Japanese claimed that the local people were willing to provide this, so why did the magistrate and the security team leader oppose it? If the bandits attacked Changli, how would the magistrate deal with it? County Magistrate Liang said that he had 30,000 self-defense troops from the people, which were enough to resist the bandits. If they could not hold out, the people of the entire county would rise up together to drive them away. The Japanese then retreated without words. After leaving the county government, they went to the Chamber of Commerce again. The content of the contact is rarely known to the outside world. After having a meal at the Chamber of Commerce at noon, they returned to Qinhuangdao.

The so-called headquarters of the East Asia Alliance United Army is now located north of Daobei in Qinhuangdao. Qi Wenping, the fake commander-in-chief, wears a kimono to work at the headquarters every day. Qi speaks fluent Japanese, and those who do not know him suspect that he is Japanese. When Qi goes out, he is always accompanied by Japanese soldiers. It is reported that their conspiracy to form a North China country is still being planned and realized. According to people from Qinhuangdao, an announcement of "New North China Government of the Republic of China" has been found in the area, and the wording is extremely absurd.

Li Jichun recently sent a team of 2,000 from Tangshan and arrived in Lanzhou by train on the 11th. That night, they went to the suburbs of Fanning in batches to proclaim the suppression of bandits. It is expected that the suppression will begin on the morning of the 13th. It is reported that when the bandit troubles in Luandong first started, Li sent a representative to Tianjin to request the provincial government to order him to suppress the bandits, but it was not approved. However, Li wanted to take this opportunity to make some achievements in order to seek future prospects, as the period for demobilization in the war zone was approaching. Therefore, he sent many representatives to station in various counties in Luandong to contact local officials, claiming that if there were occasional incidents in various places, he was willing to send a team to assist. Recently, the bandit troubles in Luandong have become more rampant, and he is even more determined to suppress them. Therefore, the provincial government granted his request. He is also willing to take responsibility for recovering Fanning. After our newly formed security team arrived, they went to Liushouying on the Beining Road to carry out the suppression of the bandits on the southern route. If the two routes attack at the same time, the bandits in Luandong will not be difficult to eliminate. I do not know whether Li has the sincerity to suppress the bandits or not. (12th)

Chen Diaoyuan Arrives in Nanchang—Zhang Qun and Others Ascend Mount Lu from Xunyang—
