Police Training Institute Recruits 300 Student Police Officers Monthly Stipend of Ten Yuan

The Municipal Public Security Bureau is actively restoring the Police Training Institute to cultivate police talent. Director Wen has appointed Li Guangzeng, inspector general of the bureau, as the director of the preparatory committee, responsible for overseeing everything. It is reported that the committee has now selected the site of the Quanzhang Middle School in the Nanshi, which has been closed, as the site of the institute, hired workers to repair it, and added school equipment. Classes will begin on a scheduled date. A notice has also been posted to recruit 300 student police officers for the 16th class. The methods are as follows: (1) Quota: 300 students. (2) Qualifications: (A) Graduate of higher primary school or equivalent academic ability. (B) Age between 20 and 30. (C) Physically strong. (D) Not sentenced to imprisonment. (E) Not a police officer dismissed by this bureau. (3) Registration: October 16 to 26, at the preparatory office of the institute at the former site of the Shanghai County Office in Penglai and at the various district general offices. (4) Length of study: Limited to six months. (5) Treatment: No tuition or uniform fees are charged. A monthly stipend of ten yuan is provided. Food expenses are deducted from the stipend. After graduation, students will be assigned to various districts to serve. (6) Examination subjects: (A) Physical examination. (B) Oral examination. (C) Written examination (Chinese, arithmetic, general knowledge). Those who fail the physical examination and oral examination will not be allowed to participate in the written examination. (7) Examination dates and addresses: Physical examination and oral examination will be held from October 30 to November 2 at the former site of the Shanghai County Office on Penglai Road. The written examination will be held at Wanzhu Elementary School in Jiumudi. Detailed regulations can be obtained at the registration office. A two-cent stamp should be attached for mail requests.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Dining Car Refuses to Sell Chinese Tea The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends a Letter to the Railway Bureau for Negotiations

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, regarding the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway dining car's refusal to sell Chinese tea, which violates the duty of promoting national products, yesterday sent a letter to the two Railway Administration Bureaus for negotiations. The original letter is recorded as follows: "To the esteemed, on the 13th of this month, we received a letter from the Hangzhou Gate Tea Association stating that the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau has been operating Qiantang Bore Tide Viewing special trains for several decades. The sales of Longjing tea leaves and West Lake lotus root powder, specialty products of Zhejiang, as well as Hangzhou-prepared snacks, have been handled by passenger car operators, which has greatly promoted production and sales. However, we have learned with great shock that this year, the Railway Bureau is operating Qiantang Bore Tide Viewing special trains, implementing a 'noble' system, not attaching third-class passenger vehicles, and prohibiting the sale of Zhejiang's special agricultural products such as Longjing tea and other food items, limiting sales to French pastries, milk, and black tea, as evidenced by railway printed orders. We believe that in modern national society, agricultural finance is the lifeline for survival. Longjing tea is a special agricultural product that has been subjected to foreign encroachment in recent years, with a significant impact. We are thinking of ways to remedy the situation, but unexpectedly, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureau's Qiantang Bore Tide Viewing special trains suddenly changed their old regulations, restricting sales of Zhejiang Longjing tea. Although the sales volume of the Qiantang Bore Tide Viewing special trains is small, it is related to the observation of people from various countries, and the promotion power is very large. If the restriction is allowed, the impact will be great, and it is not a trivial matter related to people's livelihoods. Therefore, we respectfully request that you immediately forward this to the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau for investigation and handling in accordance with the old regulations for the Qiantang Bore Tide Viewing special trains over the years, and do not be exploited by foreigners, rashly restricting the sale of foreign pastries, milk, and black tea, in order to protect the life of agricultural product Longjing tea. Regarding the sale of food and beverages on the railway cars, although it is handled by charter cars, the Railway Bureau should have the responsibility of supervision at any time. Traditionally, only hotels and public entertainment venues have taken advantage of the tendency of people to be westernized and specifically promote foreign goods, which has long been criticized by the general public. If this kind of prohibiting the sale of domestic food and beverages and limiting the sale of foreign goods is not the sole decision of the contractors, then it means that the state-run enterprise itself regards domestic goods as enemies, which is unreasonable in both emotion and logic. Therefore, we are responding by forwarding the situation. We respectfully request that your bureau promptly investigate and take effective measures to rectify the situation, to ensure public friendship."

News from the Red Swastika Society

Establishment of Additional Refugee Shelters in Ping The World Red Swastika Society previously organized two relief teams and established three temporary shelters in response to the war in Beiping to implement relief efforts. Now, it is reported that the society believes that the war in the northeast and northwest of Ping has not yet subsided, and the refugees fleeing the disaster continue to arrive. At this time when the autumn wind is biting and people are suffering from cold and hunger, yesterday, four additional shelters were set up in the suburbs of Ping, including the Fourth Shelter at Andingmen, the Fifth Shelter at Lishuiqiao Bridge, the Sixth Shelter at Jiajiayao, and the Seventh Shelter at Baishanzhuang. Lodging and food preparations are complete, and a large number of people are being sheltered. At the same time, two additional relief teams were formed, with the society's president, Wang Zhen Gui, serving as the supervising captain. Yesterday afternoon, he led more than 20 team members, police officers, and porters, carrying stretchers and medicines, to the Lishuiqiao area. Another team, led by Su Jinglin, is being prepared and organized, intending to depart immediately for Baishanzhuang and other places in the northwest of Ping to implement relief efforts.

Relief for the Jiaxiang Flood The General Headquarters of the World Red Swastika Society yesterday received a report from Cao Hengyuan, the captain of the third relief team, on the distribution of relief in the Jiaxiang flood area of Shandong Province, which stated: "We are now reporting the progress of our team's distribution in the Jiaxiang disaster area. We found that 44 villages in the first, third, and fourth districts were affected by the disaster, with 1,117 extremely poor households. The relief funds distributed this time were divided into three grades: the first grade was for households whose houses were washed away by the water, with a distribution of three yuan per household; the second and third grades were for those who could not earn a living due to the flood, with a distribution of three yuan or one yuan per household depending on the size of the household. A total of over 1,870 yuan was distributed, and the distribution was completed yesterday. Today, the team is returning to Ning, and the city of Jinning Southwest Township, which was affected by the disaster, is scheduled to be visited by the team tomorrow to distribute funds separately."

French Concession Will Have a Charity Hospital Affiliated with Guangci Hospital

The French Concession Charity Association, at a meeting of the board of directors on the 5th of this month, resolved to allocate 345,000 yuan from its public funds to build a charity medical room in Guangci Hospital, so that Chinese poor people living in the French Concession who are ill can be safely sent to the hospital for treatment. The internal layout and equipment of the hospital will be modeled after the latest-style four-story Western-style buildings. If future expansion is insufficient, the hospital can add a five-story building, which will include the following departments: a medical treatment department with 300 beds, a registration room, a dental clinic, and an emergency room. The layout of each department is complete. The Charity Association will allocate 30,000 yuan per year as annual operating expenses. For Guangci Hospital, 100 beds have been allocated, which are distributed free of charge by the Public Works Bureau to treat public patients in the concession. The French Concession Municipal Council and the management of the hospital will cooperate in the closest manner, so a management advisory committee has been established.

The personnel in charge of the association include representatives from the Jiangnan Catholic Church Hospital, the Public Works Bureau, and the Charity Association. The Charity Association is entirely dedicated to the well-being of the Chinese poor in the French Concession. The hospital is affiliated with Guangci Hospital in recognition of Guangci Hospital, which has a history of twenty-five years since its establishment and has made great achievements in the public welfare of the French Concession. The Huatong Public School, which the Charity Association founded last year on Saiposai Road, has achieved remarkable results in the past year. Although the number of classrooms has increased and can accommodate 830 students, it is still unable to accommodate all the students. The board of directors has resolved to continue setting up classrooms and expects to accommodate 1,000 students next spring.

Overview of the Flood Situation in Chongbaoqi Three Counties

Jiang Gantting, Fan Tai, and Xu Jishuang, three members of the Southern Sichuan Chongbaoqi Five Counties Flood Relief Association, recently went to Chongbaoqi three counties to investigate the actual situation in the disaster areas. The findings of the three members are recorded as follows:

Qidong

Located north of Chongming County, adjacent to Haimen on one side, and surrounded by rivers and seas on three sides, the entire county is divided into eight districts, making transportation very inconvenient. Two sudden surges of flood tide rose more than ten feet, and 90 breaches occurred on the dikes along the river and sea coasts in various districts, totaling more than 12,000 zhang. More than 20 bridges, large and small, were washed away in the tributary rivers. In the northeast coastal areas, districts seven and eight, approximately 60 li, had 40 breaches. District six along the river was also breached twice. The flood tide was rapid, and the waves were turbulent. In an instant, six or seven villages in the countryside were swept away, and two-fifths of the entire county became a flooded area. The disaster area covers an area of more than 241,000 mu, with more than 70,000 victims, most of whom are homeless. Among them, more than 350 people drowned, and more than 7,100 houses collapsed. The loss of flowers, grains, etc., amounted to more than 3 million yuan, and the price of drowned livestock was approximately 800,000 yuan. Moreover, after the affected fields were soaked by seawater salt, they will not be suitable for cultivation for three years. The direct and indirect losses cannot be counted. Recently, the weather has gradually cooled, and dozens of victims are huddled together in groups, without food or clothing, which is a tragic sight. Because Qidong is low-lying, it has suffered particularly severely.

Chongming

Located northeast of Baoshan, surrounded by rivers on all sides, the most severely affected areas are the F康 Town in the fifth district and the Beixin Village. The entire embankment was destroyed, farmland was submerged, and houses collapsed. There are approximately 9,000 victims in the district. Second, in the first district, Hongmei and other nine villages, 70-80% of the embankments were also destroyed. More than 30,000 mu of farmland were affected, and more than 1,000 houses collapsed. Statistics show that the entire county has approximately 433,000 mu of affected farmland, approximately 10,800 houses, more than 39,000 victims, and more than 200 deaths.

Baoshan

Located in the east of Jiangsu, the affected areas are Changxingsha, Dongxingsha, Ruifengsha, Dingxingsha, Shitousha, and Ping'ansha, totaling six sandbars, which are in the north of Baoshan and are divided into four villages. There are more than 25,000 mu of fields, which all produce rice and wheat. The area is shaped like a sand belt, surrounded by water on all sides, and transportation is inconvenient. There are hidden sandbars along the coast, and ships cannot dock unless the tide rises. Since 1919, it has suffered from hurricanes and floods, but this storm was huge, and many official and private embankments were breached. There are approximately 10,000 victims, 2,800 houses collapsed and were washed away, 29 people drowned, and the loss of rice and grain was approximately more than 100,000 yuan. The households in this village are mostly guest籍, mostly from Beisha. After the disaster, there was no harvest, and many went to other places to seek a living.

Summary of Continued Emergency Relief in Chuansha

After the China Jisheng Association organized the first emergency relief effort in Yuanyuan Sandbar in Chuansha, it organized a second relief effort yesterday. Mr. Mu Jiaxuan was again appointed as the director and set off again. Another 200 shi of relief rice, 2,500 bamboo poles for building sheds, tens of thousands of jin of rice straw, and hundreds of cotton-padded clothes were transported to the disaster area for relief. However, the disaster is large, and the rice is scarce, making it difficult to cover the entire area. It is hoped that all kind-hearted people and those concerned about their hometowns will continue to provide assistance so that the stranded fish can recover slightly and not all die in the ditch.

Frequent Labor Strikes in British and American Factories The Three-Factory Work Stoppage May Resume Work Tomorrow The First and Second Factories' Termination of Fees Caused Disputes

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, after the workers of the British-American Factory No. 3 on Taopeng Road went on strike on the afternoon of the 13th to protest the factory's recognition of the labor union and other demands, the Social Affairs Bureau considered it inappropriate and instructed the cigarette union in District Four to stop it. It was also scheduled for discussions on the 17th, and it is expected that work will resume today. Unexpectedly, the new and old factories rejected the labor union's collection of membership fees, and after unsuccessful negotiations with the union, disputes are about to arise again. The union is scheduled to hold a representatives' meeting to respond, and will submit a request to the Party and government for a ban, as well as request revisions to the management methods and labor-management mutual aid conditions. The detailed information is recorded as follows:

Factory Labor Strike at Three Factories

Following criticism from the Social Affairs Bureau regarding the labor strike at the Anglo-American Third Factory on Taopeng Road, the Fourth District Cigarette Workers' Union dispatched Executive Director Zhou Xuexiang to mediate. Work resumed successively as a result, awaiting the Social Affairs Bureau's mediation on the 17th. However, the workers insisted on their demands, which remained unresolved. Consequently, the General Labor Union assigned Executive Director Zhou Xuexiang to continue mediating. As yesterday was a regular weekly holiday, it was expected that work would resume as usual this morning. However, workers expressed that if mediation proves ineffective, they are determined to continue their opposition.

Refusal to Collect Membership Dues

The labor dispute at the Anglo-American First and Second Factories in Pudong was temporarily resolved through mediation by Party and government authorities. Unexpectedly, the factory management recently violated the mediation agreement by refusing to pay wages for the strike period and posting notices prohibiting the collection of membership dues. They threatened to dismiss any worker found collecting dues. Upon hearing this, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, citing the long-standing practice of collecting membership dues without prior objection from the factory, deemed this a deliberate attempt to undermine the labor movement. In addition to petitioning the Municipal Government for intervention, they also sent Chen Peide, Lou Jingguan, Zhang Yuping, and others to the factory for unsuccessful negotiations yesterday.

Proposed Conditions

After the union representatives' unsuccessful negotiations, they formally proposed five methods for collecting dues in writing: (1) Dues collection should continue according to existing practices; (2) If the factory cannot accommodate this, it should follow the example of the British-owned Xiang Sheng Iron Factory and the Hua Cheng Tobacco Factory by deducting dues on a monthly basis; (3) If the factory cannot accommodate even this, the union should send representatives to the factory monthly to collect dues next to the wage disbursement table; (4) Dues collection should be limited to union members; (5) Workers responsible for collecting dues should be granted temporary leave, always with the principle of not hindering the factory's operations.

Delegates' Congress

Unexpectedly, the factory did not provide a satisfactory response to the union's letter, and negotiations reached a standstill. The factory even posted a notice claiming that workers reported the ban on dues collection. The union considered this a deliberate provocation. In addition to petitioning the Party and government authorities for impartial intervention, they scheduled an emergency delegates' congress to discuss countermeasures. On the 15th of this month, dues collection will continue as usual. Furthermore, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, noting that their demands for revising management rules and labor-management mutual aid conditions have not been met, leaving workers bound by the original terms, specifically dispatched Chen Peide, Lou Jingguan, Zhang Yuping, Xiao Gengsheng, and others to the Municipal Government to petition for prompt revisions to prevent further unrest.

Official Document to the Party and Government

The Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union submitted a document to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau, stating that the factory's obstruction of dues collection necessitates prompt mediation to maintain union affairs. The document stated that the union's monthly dues collection has been conducted by representatives, without objection from the factory, since its establishment. However, the factory recently posted a notice claiming it was acting under the Social Affairs Bureau's orders to prohibit dues collection and threatening to dismiss any worker found collecting dues. It also falsely claimed to be acting on worker reports, deliberately sowing discord. The union, based on worker reports, proposed five methods for collecting dues (omitted) to the factory, seeking a compromise. However, the factory completely rejected them. Further negotiations with the factory also failed. The union's monthly expenses and unemployment benefits for workers rely entirely on membership dues. If these are stopped, the union will inevitably collapse. The union has been collecting dues for many years, and this practice has never been changed. It does not hinder the factory's operations, so there is no reason to prohibit it. If the factory proceeds to dismiss workers who collect dues, it will inevitably trigger a major upheaval. Therefore, it urgently reported to the authorities, requesting prompt and impartial mediation to maintain union affairs and quell the unrest.

No Changes in the Electric Company Labor Strike Yesterday, Some Say All Chinese Employees Will Return to Work This Morning, But the Lianyi Society Absolutely Denies It

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that the strike by Chinese employees of the Shanghai Electric Company has lasted nearly half a month. Because the labor and management opinions have not reached a consensus, it is difficult to resolve urgently. Since the company lured a small number of Chinese employees to return to work, yesterday happened to be a weekly holiday, and the employees of various departments still insisted on striking, and there were no changes. The Shanghai Electric Company Colleagues' Lianyi Society, in addition to persuading the more than 30 people who were lured by the company to return to work to act together, will issue a notice to members to unanimously reject the Electric Company's enticement methods in order to consolidate unity. However, on the other hand, news came out that all Chinese employees will return to work this morning. However, the Lianyi Society said that the news was not certain and absolutely denied it. Let's record it to wait for confirmation.

Introduction by the Preparatory Committee of the Tramp Factory, the Owed Wages of the Tramps' Work Are Being Sued, the Court Will Hear the Case This Morning

The China Tramp Factory was initiated by more than 20 people, including Chou Gao Chen Yaoqing, Mao Guanhao, and Zhu Muyun, in February of this year, and was approved by the Municipal Government. The committee introduced more than 80 tramps, including Lu Jingren, to Tian Shende Sauce Factory and other places in the city for sales. This Morning on Bailer Road, Hengqing Lane, Ruthless Bandits Shot and Killed Chinese and Western Detectives, Both Sides Fired More Than 100 Shots for an Hour, Western Detectives from the French Concession and Detectives from the Public Security Bureau Died - Two Injured, Two Bandits, One Fled and One Arrested -

At 2:00 this morning, our reporter learned that a bandit resisting arrest and killing a French Concession Western detective and a Public Security Bureau detective occurred at No. 14 Hengqing Lane at the end of Bailer Road in the French Concession. He rushed to inquire and recorded the details as follows: First, Lu Ying, the captain of the Criminal Investigation Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, received a secret report from an informant that a pavilion room at No. 14 Hengqing Lane at the end of Bailer Road South of Route Lafayette in the French Concession,

Was Hiding a Notorious Bandit

Captain Lu then dispatched detectives Liu Changrui, Chen Liangfu, Gong Hexiang, etc., and led detectives to the General Police Station of the French Concession at about 11:00 last night to request that personnel be dispatched to go together to make the arrest. The police chief immediately dispatched many capable Chinese and Western detectives, etc., and set off for No. 14 Hengqing Lane, knocked on the door and entered. At this time, there were two bandits in the pavilion room. One bandit knew that things were not good, and immediately

Fled Along the Roof

The other bandit was too late to escape, and immediately closed the door to resist arrest. The bandit was extremely fierce and held a box cannon in each hand, firing at the Chinese and Western detectives, etc. Both sides fired more than 100 shots. The entire neighborhood was shocked for a while. Because the position of the escalator was very small and not enough to expand, the bandit held on

With the Determination of a Cornered Beast

The detectives were unable to enter the room and held each other for as long as an hour. In the fierce battle, bullets flew horizontally. A French Concession detective (name not yet ascertained) was shot and killed. Gong Hexiang, a detective from the Public Security Bureau, was also shot and killed in a vital part. Liu Changrui was shot twice, Chen Liangshe was shot in the chest, and his left arm was broken. Another Western detective was shot twice and injured. Until the bullets ran out,

The Bandit Was Arrested

The remaining Chinese and Western detectives who arrived on the scene will send the wounded and killed detectives, etc., to the court this morning to apply for a ruling. In this battle, one bandit resisted arrest and killed two lives. It lasted for a long time. It can be said that it is a rare event. The ferocity of the bandit can also be seen here.

Zhang Yuanruo Gives a Radio Speech, Titled "The Self-Salvation Movement of the Chinese Nation"

The 5th National Goods Movement Conference in this city is sponsored by the Social Affairs Bureau of the Municipal Government and has already opened on October 10. In order to make citizens understand the significance of the national goods movement and arouse citizens' patriotic thoughts, the conference also gave radio speeches at the Greater China Radio Station on Nanjing Road. At 11:00 a.m. today, the conference hired Mr. Zhang Yuanruo to give a speech entitled [The Self-Salvation Movement of the Chinese Nation]. The content is divided into six main points: (1) The principle of modern national survival; (2) The real crisis of the Chinese nation; (3) Promoting national goods is the self-salvation of the Chinese nation; (4) Psychological obstacles to the national goods movement; (5) Contradictory phenomena in the national goods movement; (6) Methods to promote the national goods movement. Mr. Zhang has always paid attention to and advocated the national salvation movement. It is expected that he will have a wonderful and practical speech at that time.

Truck Breaks Cable, Large Chimney Falls and Kills Three People

No. 13 Yichang Road, West Shanghai, was formerly the Fuyuanji Paper Shop, but it has now been relocated. It was founded by soy sauce merchants and is the Yiji Soy Sauce Essence Factory. Therefore, the soy sauce wooden barrels in the factory all have the "Zhang Chongxin" signboard. At about 11:45 yesterday morning, a No. 16912 truck belonging to the Huang Fuji Freight Car Company on Zhaofeng Road, Hongkou, loaded with a large number of wooden boards, was driving through the area. Because the truck was loaded too high, the iron wire tied to the iron sheet chimney on the roof broke. As a result, the chimney was broken immediately and fell down, injuring three workers in the car on the spot, including Zhang Fusheng, 28 years old, from Shaoxing, who was injured in the waist; Zhou Shaorong, 30 years old, from Ningbo, who was injured in the waist and feet; and Wu Agui, 26 years old, from Jiangbei, who was injured in the waist and abdomen. The street police rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm, copied the car number, and reported it to the police station for investigation. The three injured people were quickly sent to the Renji Hospital for treatment.

Hongshun Mutual Aid Society Called Group Leaders for Training Yesterday

The Shanghai Hongshun Mutual Aid Society has recently increased the number of members and the affairs of the society are becoming increasingly complex. At 8:00 p.m. the night before last, all group leaders were specially called for training. More than 60 group leaders attended. Chairman Wu Zichang and recorder Zhao Yunpu performed the ceremony. The chairman announced the purpose of the meeting and the responsibilities of each group leader, hoping that the group leaders would work hard to collect membership white money fees. The relocation of members' houses should be investigated, reported, and corrected. Next, former chairman Yang Wendao reported the reasons for resigning from the chairman of the committee, saying briefly that he was unable to take care of both public and private affairs, so he resigned from the position of chairman. Comrade Wu Yuchang was elected to act on his behalf and take responsibility. He hoped that all the group leaders would obey the guidance of Chairman Wu. As for himself, he is still an executive committee member. For the affairs of the society, he will still do his best to fulfill his responsibility if he can take care of them, and hoped that the members would be informed and not misunderstood. The society has now appointed Yang Daxuan, Pu Fengming, and Yang Zhijian as instructors. The three comrades have knowledge, experience, and perseverance. Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory forecast the weather at 4:30 p.m. yesterday, saying that the sky was dark, and there were strong seasonal winds along the coast of the country. The hurricane east of the Philippines would move north, and the low-pressure center southwest-west of the Ogasawara Islands would also move north or northeast. The weather was bad southeast of Miyako Island and Okinawa. The center of the hurricane was at 2:00 p.m., one within 120 miles of the intersection of 17 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude, and the other within 120 miles of the intersection of 26 degrees north latitude and 139 degrees east longitude. The wind force was not known. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 74.7 and the lowest was 59.2. On the same day last year, the highest was 78.8 and the lowest was 53.2.

Shen Bao National Games Special Edition, No. 7

Sixth Day of the National Games: Shanghai Wins All-Around Championship Again; Zhang Lingjia Sets New National Record in Decathlon; Guangdong Team Sets New National Record in 4x100m Relay; Shanghai Women's Basketball Team Beats Fujian, Championship Hopeful; Men's and Women's Swimming Competitions Begin Today

(Nanjing, 15th) Today is the sixth day of the National Games. The all-around championship went to Shanghai again. National records were broken in the decathlon and 4x100m relay. The ball games are tense. In the Shanghai-Fujian women's basketball game, Shanghai won by one point. The all-around competition is over. Men's and women's swimming start this morning.

Guangdong Sets New National Record in 4x100m Relay Final; 44.4 Seconds Even Better Than Preliminary Round; Shanghai Second, Beijing Third, Beiping Fourth; Shanghai Failed Due to Second Leg

(Nanjing, 15th) In the 4x100m relay final of the all-around competition, Liaoning withdrew. Shanghai, Beiping, Guangdong, Hebei, and Beijing competed for the win. Guangdong won with a time of 44.4 seconds, a new national record. Shanghai was second, Beijing was third, and Beiping was fourth. Shanghai lost ground in the first two legs. Beiping led all the way but unfortunately hesitated during the final baton exchange, resulting in fourth place. Guangdong won in the final leg. Shanghai was two meters behind, and Hao Chunde and Cheng Jinguan were frustrated for failing to win the championship.

Fu Bao Lu Sets New National Record in Decathlon Pole Vault; 3.85 Meters Even Better

(Nanjing, 15th) Fu Baolu broke the national record again in the pole vault of the decathlon today. The result was even better at 3.85 meters.

Overview of Decathlon

(Nanjing, 15th) Zhang Lingjia set a new national record in the decathlon. Chen Ling of Shanghai also broke the national record. In the second half of the decathlon competition, Zhang Lingjia of Beiping won the decathlon with 5889.587 points. Chen Ling of Shanghai was the runner-up, also scoring 5607.605 points. The results of the top two both broke the national record held by Liu Renxiu. Chen Baoqiu of Shanghai was third, and although he did not participate in the pole vault, he still scored 5408.105 points, which was close to the national record. Cao Baoyu of Shanghai was fourth with a score of 5248.75. Chen Baoqiu initially led in the first half of the competition. However, in the second half, he did not score in the pole vault. Otherwise, Chen's performance would have been unstoppable. Here is an overview of the top six: (1) Zhang Lingjia is a veteran of the decathlon in China. It is said that Liu Renxiu abandoned the competition in the first half, and Zhang already had the championship in his hands. Zhang got 11.7 seconds in the 100 meters, which was beyond his own expectations. Zhang, who weighs over 180 kilograms, has never had such a result. Among the last five events, Zhang is a thrower in high jump, discus, and javelin. He even got 443 points in the pole vault, which he is not good at. However, in the 400 meters of the first five events, he only ran 57 seconds in the dark. His usual result is 55 seconds. If everything could go as planned, he could be expected to exceed 6500 points. (2) Chen Ling excels in running and jumping in all events, but his throwing skills are slightly worse. The 100 meters, high jump, and pole vault are the reasons for Chen's victory. He scored over 800 points in the high jump and over 700 points in the 100 meters and pole vault. However, his score in the three throwing events was too low, which is why Chen is not as good as Zhang. (3) Chen Baoqiu is the opposite of Chen Ling. He is good at throwing but bad at pole vault. He only tried one jump and fell into the pit with the pole, causing the whole audience to laugh. Chen refused to jump again and gave up. If Chen did not have this shortcoming, no one would be able to beat him. (4) Cao Yu is an old general and the champion of the previous competition. His hopes for this competition are very weak. Cao's efforts are definitely not inferior to others. His score also relies on running, jumping, and high jump, which is unexpected. (5) Zhao Enji was originally a famous decathlete in North China, but he failed due to the pentathlon, leading to his defeat. Zhao took the lead in the high jump race. The 100 meters, long jump, high jump, and 400 meters are also Zhao's scoring events, but the three throwing events are too bad. Otherwise, he could have been selected. (6) Fu Baolu's participation in the decathlon is not to win the championship, but to make up for his pole vault. Fu broke the national record in the pole vault final with 3.75 meters a few days ago, but because it was dark, he could not jump again, so he gave up. On the 15th, Fu focused on this event in the decathlon. Fu jumped over 3.40 meters, 3.50 meters, 3.60 meters, and 3.70 meters. When he raised it to 3.85 meters, he also jumped over it in one try. Then the referee raised it to 4 meters. Fu did not have this strength, so he requested to set it at 3.95 meters. If he could jump over this height, he could equal 1000 points of the world's decathlon pole vault record. In the first jump, his hand slightly touched the crossbar and caused the pole to fall. The second jump was a step. The third jump was successful, and the audience couldn't help but shout. Unfortunately, the wind blew the pole to the ground, which was a great pity. The official result was only 3.85 meters, but it was still amazing. Judging from Fu's posture, it will not be difficult to jump over 4 meters in the near future, and he can get a position in the Far Eastern Games.

Hao Chunde's Pentathlon Did Not Break the Far Eastern Record; The 9th Far Eastern Games Still Used the Old Scoring Method; The Current New Scoring Method Has Different Algorithms; Hao and Wang Are Still Far Behind with the New Scoring Method; This Newspaper Exclusively Noted Yesterday

(Nanjing, 15th) In the pentathlon, Hao Chunde and Wang Jihuai of Shanghai won the championship and runner-up, respectively. The fact that their scores exceeded 3000 points shocked the country and is indeed a valuable harvest for the track and field community in China in recent times. At the same time, after this record was discovered, newspapers in Beijing, Shanghai, and other places all used the largest fonts as headlines, claiming that this record broke the Far Eastern record, and even the special edition of the Games also published it in this way, which is laughable due to a lack of knowledge. The highest record created by Kosaku Sumiyoshi of Japan in the 9th Far Eastern Games was 2838 points, which is indeed less than the total score of Hao and Wang this time, but it must be known that the scoring methods are different. The 9th Far Eastern Games used the old scoring method, and now the new scoring method has been adopted. The old and new algorithms are different. The old one is less, and the new one is more. If the Far Eastern record of 2838 points is calculated using the new method, it will be around 3500 points, and Hao and Wang are still far behind. This kind of error is really a joke. Only this newspaper made a special note on the 15th, but the official promotional materials of the Games are still spreading the error.

The 10,000-Meter Dispute Comes to an End

Maintaining the Resolution of the Joint Conference; The Judging Committee Held a Meeting Yesterday and Resolved; Jiangsu Will Maintain Sportsmanship and No Longer Protest; The Judgment Is Officially Released, and the Results Are Canceled

(Nanjing, 15th) The Judging Committee held a meeting on the morning of the 15th and decided to uphold the resolution of the Joint Competition and Judging Conference. Later, Zhang Dongping, the leader of the Jiangsu delegation, said that in order to maintain sportsmanship, Jiangsu Province could no longer protest the 10,000-meter decision according to law. This is an error in the duty of the referee of the Games. In the future, other legal methods will be used to ask colleagues in the sports community to jointly study the 10,000-meter judgment process.

The Judgment Is Officially Released

(Nanjing, 15th) Zhang Boling, the chief referee, officially released the judgment on the 10,000-meter race, saying that according to the resolution of the joint meeting of the 14th Competition Committee and the Judging Committee, the number 180 athlete participating in the 10,000-meter race was invalid. Therefore, this chief referee judges that in the 10,000-meter race, the first place is number 13, the second place is number 284, the third place is number 16, and the fourth place is number 15, but there are no official results.

Rejecting Jiangsu's Protest

(Nanjing, 15th) The Judging Committee convened a meeting at the Central Hotel at 9:00 a.m. on the 15th to discuss the Jiangsu delegation's letter of protest against the 10,000-meter judgment. Chairman Zhang Boling ruled that the grounds for the protest were unfounded and sent a letter to Zhang Dongping, the leader of the Jiangsu delegation, saying that after receiving your team's letter of protest regarding the 10,000 meters, this team convened a meeting on the morning of the 15th and refuted it item by item. The clauses are listed as follows: (1) This committee did not deny that Mr. Huang Shibin was an official lap counter. The statement that the lap count was inaccurate was an error admitted by Mr. Huang himself, so this protest cannot be established. (2) The chief referee's announcement that 180 was the first place was based on the verbal report of lap counter Huang Bobin, but the next day, his lap count sheet showed that number 180 had run 21 laps. At that time, Mr. Huang admitted that the record was wrong and stated that (if other lap counters can take responsibility, the report can be invalidated). Later, it was found that Jun Wenchang was ordered to record and was also responsible for stating that number 180 had only run 19 laps, one lap short, and there was a lap count sheet to prove it, so this protest cannot be established. (3) On the conference lap sheets, the numbers from 20 onwards were generally crossed out with a horizontal line, but on the lap sheet used by Mr. Huang, the numbers up to 20 and the number 1 were marked with an X, and the strength and color of the writing on the number 21 were exactly the same as those recorded on other numbers. This is enough to prove that his record was wrong, so this protest cannot be established. (4) During the 10,000-meter race, Committee Member Wang Zhengting watched from the east command platform and had no responsibility for formal recording, but according to his unofficial observation, from the second lap to the ninth lap, number 180 was not seen in the leading group, but from the tenth lap onwards, number 180 was seen in the leading group. According to the report of lap counter Li Wenchang, number 180 was one lap behind in the first ten laps, so this protest cannot be established. (5) This committee uses official reports as records. News reports should not be used as evidence, so this clause cannot be established. The above clauses have been reviewed by this committee in a meeting and deemed to be unfounded. Therefore, the resolution of the previous Competition Committee and Judging Committee joint meeting should still be implemented, and according to the provisions of Article 20 of the Competition Regulations, the protest fee should be confiscated, etc. A receipt for the protest deposit of ten yuan is attached. According to Zhang Dongping, if possible during the Games, he plans to invite the Jin athlete who competed in the 10,000 meters to perform an informal public performance with Jin Zhongkang to prove Jin Gu's strength.

Soccer

The Dispute Between Shanghai and Liaoning Soccer Teams Will Be Handled by the Judging Committee; After Shanghai Won 6-0 Against Liaoning, Jiang Shan Jing and Li Bairen Suddenly Brawled; The Order Was Disrupted, and the Game Was Stopped; The Liaoning Instructor Said the Record Should Be Canceled - Hong Kong Won 3-1 Against Beiping - It Is Not Easy to Win Against Strong Opponents

(Nanjing, 15th) At 4:00 p.m. on the 15th, in the soccer match between Shanghai and Liaoning, referee Zhou Jiaqi, the Liaoning team was very strong. When they took to the field, they were flying all over the place. The Shanghai team had a hard time dealing with them. Moreover, Liaoning was in a favorable position with the wind, and their attacks often hovered near the Shanghai team's goal. Zhou's goal was to deal with it on both sides. Jiang Shan Jing's footwork was inaccurate, Xu Yahui was often robbed of the ball, and Li Yichen and Chen Jiaqiu couldn't kick the ball. The unexpected good performance of the Liaoning team was met with continuous cheers from the audience. In the third minute of the kickoff, Li Yichen took the ball and kicked it into the net within the inner defense, opening the scoring. After that, both sides fought fiercely for a long time without winning or losing. At 15 minutes, Liaoning committed a foul and was penalized with a 12-yard penalty kick, which Sun Jin converted into a goal. The Liaoning army did not lose heart and resisted to the end. At one point, they sent troops to attack. Once, Zhou Xianyan caught the ball, but due to the strong wind and rapid ball, he lost his grip, and the ball flew into the net, only an inch away from going in. Otherwise, it would have been dangerous. The Shanghai team also retaliated, with Wan Xianghua and Li Yichen each scoring a goal. The first half ended with a score of 4-0.

Fighting Broke Out, and the Game Was Suspended

In the second half, the teams switched sides and continued to fight. Liaoning was facing a headwind, making it even more difficult to cope. The Shanghai team replaced Luo Haiguang with Chen Hongguang. Chen's foot was hard and accurate, and he scored two more goals. Although Liaoning was defeated, they still launched a full-scale counterattack. With 16 minutes remaining in the second half, Liaoning's center forward dribbled straight into the heart of the Shanghai defense. Because the Shanghai defenders were surrounding him very closely, he kicked the ball to the left corner. Liaoning's left forward, Li Bairen, rushed to catch up, but the referee quickly blew the silver whistle for offside. Li did not pay attention and continued to kick the ball as before. Seeing the critical situation, Jiang Shanjing, the left inner guard of Shanghai, also rushed to intercept, but accidentally kicked Li's leg. Li thought it was intentional use of violence, so he punched and attacked. Jiang also fought back, and they twisted into a ball. The referee blew his whistle repeatedly and hugged Li. At that time, armed military police gathered around and forcibly dragged Li away. The audience also poured into the field, and some even planned to join the battle group. The situation was turbulent, and there was a sense of blaming the referee. Seeing that the order was disrupted and that his own reputation was in danger, Zhou Jiaqi announced the suspension of the game. According to Zhou, the details of the incident will be reported to the Judging Committee for fair handling. The Liaoning instructor said that since the referee has announced the suspension of the game, any records of this game should be canceled. His team can only listen to the fair resolution of the Games.

Zhou Jiaqi's Report

(Nanjing, 15th) Zhou Jiaqi, the referee of the Shanghai-Liaoning soccer game, wrote to the Competition Committee on the 15th, saying that in the second soccer game between Shanghai and Liaoning at 4:00 p.m. on the 15th, he served as the referee for the game. The result of the first half was 4-0, with Shanghai taking the lead. During the game, due to the rough kicking of a certain team, six irregular actions occurred throughout the game. Although he repeatedly penalized and warned, it was still ineffective. Sixteen minutes before the end of the game, the left wing of the Liaoning team violated the offside rule, so he blew his whistle to penalize. However, the left inner forward of the Liaoning team still did not stop his movement (the left inner forward was indeed number 14) and still rushed up and deliberately kicked the right back of the Shanghai team. Both sides clashed. He stepped forward to hug the assailant, and the player (Liaoning number 14) did not take any other actions. However, the players and spectators on both sides joined in the fight, and the order was disrupted. Fortunately, the military police were present and showed off their guns to threaten them, so no bloodshed occurred. However, this unfortunate incident has already occurred, and the players on both sides have a deep sense of animosity. If the game continues, there may be more unexpected disasters. Therefore, he announced on the spot (the game will not continue today). Moreover, the Liaoning team players refused to hand over the penalty, and he was unable to collect it. This is the reason why he cannot know the name of the number 14 player. He has made a detailed report on what happened at the time, hoping that the Competition Committee will decide what to do. This is submitted to the Competition Committee.

Mayor Wu Attends Soccer Game

(Nanjing, 15th) In the afternoon of the 15th, the two soccer games between Hong Kong and Beiping and Shanghai and Liaoning were very exciting. There were nearly 10,000 spectators, and the stands and surrounding areas were full. This is a record for the soccer field. The order was quite chaotic. Wu Tiecheng, Yang Hu, and others also went to watch and stood for a long time before leaving.

Hong Kong Defeats Beiping in Three Games; The Result Is 3-1; 3-0 in the First Half

(Nanjing, 15th) In the soccer game between Hong Kong and Beiping at 2:00 p.m. on the 15th, Hong Kong won 3-1 and obtained the right to replay. Referee Chen Jixiang, in terms of strength, Hong Kong is more aggressive than Beiping, but Beiping's fighting spirit is very commendable.

Too Eager to Win, Involving Roughness

After the start of the war, the battle was fierce for a long time without winning or losing. The ball sometimes hovered in the square, with many dangerous situations. At 20 minutes, the Hong Kong center forward got the ball and went straight into the inner defense line, scoring a goal single-handedly, making the first contribution. After five minutes, Huang Meishun got the ball again. The Beiping team tried hard to counterattack, and the shouts shook far and wide. At that time, the actions of the Hong Kong army were quite rough. The left inner forward of Beiping, Fang Gechun, was injured and left the field. The Beiping goalkeeper was also punched by the Hong Kong army. At this time, the whole field was in an uproar, thinking that the actions were barbaric and should be warned. After the referee persuaded them to stop, the game continued. The Beiping army repeatedly counterattacked, but they were all waved out of bounds by Bao Gangmen. In the last ten minutes, the Hong Kong right forward got the ball and passed it to Zhou, the center forward, who gently kicked it, and it fell into the net again. The first half was 3-0, and Hong Kong won. During the break, a photographer asked the Hong Kong team to take a photo. The audience suddenly poured into the field. A person in a Sun Yat-sen suit shouted that the Hong Kong team was barbaric and did not deserve to compete, let alone take photos of them. The words were激昂 and there were loud shouts and beatings. The Hong Kong team's attitude at that time was very poor, saying that everything would follow the referee's orders, and finally, no incident occurred.

Courage to Correct Mistakes and Peaceful Victory

In the second half, the Hong Kong army changed to a defensive posture and did not抢球 very aggressively. The actions of the square were excessive. The inner guard injured Zheng Jiliang, the center forward of Hong Kong, and then left the field. The Hong Kong army was careful and courageous to correct their mistakes. The audience also gradually calmed down. At 30 minutes, the Hong Kong team was penalized with a 12-yard penalty kick, which was converted into a goal by Tang Guoliang of Beiping. Since then, Hong Kong has adopted a perfunctory extension policy. Although Beiping was lazy to counterattack, it was ultimately impenetrable due to its tight defense. In addition, Bao Gangmen was虎视眈眈 and saved 11 dangerous balls, unable to cross the line for even one step. The second half was 1-0, and Beiping won. The total score was 3-1, and the Hong Kong army won the right to replay.

Spectator Loses Manner and Provokes Emotions

(Nanjing, 15th) Most spectators do not understand the truth and shout loudly, and some even call for others to show obvious one-sided protection, which is close to provoking the emotions of the two teams. I hope the conference will pay attention to this point. In the initial battle between Hong Kong and Beiping, the Hong Kong team was eager to move forward and was slightly激列. The 后塲 was absolutely peaceful, so there was no talk of barbarism.

All Athletes Paid Respects at the Mausoleum Yesterday Morning

Athletes Paid Respects at the Mausoleum Yesterday Morning

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) At 6 AM on the 15th, all athletes, managers, and the chief leader, with their respective unit flags in formation, led by Chu Minyi and Zhang Xinfu, walked to the Mausoleum of the Premier. Arriving at the altar platform at 7 AM, they held a memorial ceremony, sang the party song, saluted, and presented three wreaths: one from all staff members of the conference, two from the chief leaders and supervisors and managers, and three from all athletes. After the wreath presentation, the inner gate of the mausoleum was opened, and all followed the path into the mausoleum for a visit. At 8 AM, they posed for a group photo on the platform and returned to the field.

The Conference Was Chaotic All Day Yesterday; The Future of the Conference Is Deeply Worrying; It Is Sincerely Hoped That the Authorities Will Pay Attention

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) On the 15th, the chaos continued, especially the assault by soldiers of the 88th Division and the disputes on the football field were even greater. The cause of the disputes on the football field was actually due to the audience's prejudice against the Shanghai team. Because Shanghai has won the all-around athletics championship and other titles, and also occupies a superior position in various ball games, it has aroused jealousy from all sides. Whenever the Shanghai team plays, there are unconscious shouts, especially the Liaoning players, who do not forget their motherland even in defeat, which aroused the sympathy of the masses. As for the skills of the Liaoning football team, they are indeed quite impressive, and their performance has improved a lot. We, with an impartial attitude, congratulate the winners and encourage the losers. We should be proud when we win and not be humiliated when we lose. Now the athletes cannot encourage themselves with this, but only care about winning or losing, to the point of acting impulsively, which is a loss of the original spirit of competition. The same incident occurred in the match between Ping and Hong Kong in football. It is truly a great misfortune for the conference and a misfortune for the sports community. Once this trend starts, the ball game playoffs in the last three days of the conference are deeply worrying. The aftermath of the Jie Zhou National Games has not subsided, and it is sincerely hoped that the conference will pay attention to seeking a satisfactory conclusion.

Women's Basketball

The Most Exciting Scene in Women's Basketball; Shanghai Defeats Fujian 26-25 to Secure a Spot in the Semifinals; Once This Hurdle Is Cleared, Shanghai's Hopes Are Endless; Shanghai Breaks Through From Despair

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) The women's basketball semifinal between Shanghai and Fujian was held at the women's basketball court at 9 AM on the 15th. The two sides were evenly matched and competed fiercely, making it one of the most exciting scenes in women's basketball since the start of the games. The score was 11-11 in the first half. In the second half, the Fujian team initially took the lead, but the Shanghai team was fortunate to have Chen Rongming score consecutive long shots, ultimately winning 26-25. In the second game between Hebei and Harbin, the Hebei team was strong, while the Harbin team's defense was weak. The difference between the two sides was too great. Hebei led 28-10 in the first half. In the second half, the Harbin team became even more unsustainable, resulting in a 63-16 victory for Hebei.

Shanghai Narrowly Defeats Fujian; 26-25, One Point More; Will Compete with Hebei for the Finals

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) Women's basketball, semifinal, the first match between Fujian and Shanghai, the strength of both sides is strong, no different from a final match.

Fujian's Momentum Is Strong

The guards of both teams are good, defending legally, with neither side making any gains. After a long time, Chen Rongming of Shanghai repeatedly missed good opportunities, and Fujian took advantage of this. Center Chen Rongtang, Xue Pixia, and You Huifang made three wonderful contributions, taking a 6-0 lead. Chen Rongming pulled back a point through a free throw opportunity. Liu Mali committed a foul, and Xue Pixia scored another point. In the first quarter, Fujian won 7-1.

Shanghai Is Like a Fish in Water

In the second quarter, Shanghai put Chen Jucai and Shi Duanxia on the court, and they did indeed win a goal. Chen Rongtang of Fujian returned the favor. Yang Sen entered the game, and Shanghai's forwards were like fish in water. Chen Jucai, Yang Sen, and Chen Rongming scored five consecutive points. Shanghai was only one point behind. Fujian shouted for a break, changing tactics. Shanghai still gained the upper hand, 11-9, turning defeat into victory. In an instant, Chen Rongtang made a long shot from afar, hitting the target, 11-11, evenly split, ending the first half.

Fujian Makes a Comeback

In the second half, Xue Pixia and You Huifang scored six consecutive points, their momentum suddenly surging. Liu Mali was replaced by Chen Rongming, and Shanghai gained this new force. Chen Jucai also pulled back two points. Unfortunately, You Huifang and Chen Rongtang made continuous gains. In the third quarter, Fujian led 12-3 by a wide margin.

Shanghai Wins by One Point

In the fourth quarter, Chen Rongming and Pan Yueying reappeared, and Shanghai improved slightly. Yang Sen, Pan Yueying, and Chen Rongming fought to break through and score. Shanghai was only two points behind at 24-22. Chen Rongming scored another two points, tying the score again at 24-24. Chen Duanping committed a foul, and Chen Rongtang scored the free throw, putting Shanghai one point behind. Chen Rongming made the final contribution, and Shanghai won Fujian 26-25. It was indeed a narrow victory.

Hebei Defeats Harbin 63-16; Will Meet Shanghai in the Semifinals

In the second women's basketball game, Hebei played against Harbin. The Harbin team was slow to act and far from being their opponent. Hebei's play was very commendable.

Harbin Weakens as Soon as They Enter the Court

At the start of the game, Hebei scored a point, and the Harbin team immediately slumped. Jin Shuji's jade arms stretched out, scoring frequently. Harbin team's Wang Baorong and Zhang Shufen barely managed to score four points. Hebei team won the first quarter sixteen to four. In the second quarter, Harbin team performed better, but Hebei was still better overall, winning the first half 28 to 10.

Jin Shuquan Becomes More Agile

Starting in the second half, Hebei's Jin Shuquan became even more agile, charging left and right, unstoppable. Harbin team only managed to score two points from two free throws. At the end of the third quarter, Hebei had 49 points, and Harbin had 12. In the fourth quarter, the Harbin team became more and more isolated, making it difficult to resist. The Hebei team sailed smoothly, Jin Shuquan was steady and extraordinary, and finally won sixty-three to sixteen.

Women's Tennis

Shanghai, Sichuan, and Shanxi Enter the Semifinals; Starts on the 17th

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) The second round of women's tennis has ended, with Shanghai, Shanxi, Sichuan, and Beiping securing spots in the semifinals. Starting at 2 PM on the 15th, the women's tennis competition continues. The second round has all concluded, resulting in Shanghai winning all three matches against Anhui, and Shanxi and Sichuan each eliminating Beijing and Hebei with a score of 2-1. After the rounds in the second round were decided, Shanghai, Shanxi, and Sichuan all secured spots in the semifinals, which will take place on the 17th.

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) In the second round of women's tennis, Shanghai's Mao Yuwen, Anhui's Liu Yufang, and Sichuan's Bao Dajing defeated Hebei's Cui Shuzhen, and Shanxi's Wang Chunjing defeated Beijing's Liu Yulan. There are seven units that have secured a spot in the second round: Shanghai, Anhui, Sichuan, Hebei, Shanxi, Beijing, and Beiping. The competition began at 9 AM on the 15th, with the first singles match being Shanghai vs. Anhui, Sichuan vs. Hebei, Shanxi vs. Beijing, and Beiping having a bye. As a result, Shanghai, Sichuan, and Shanxi each won a singles match.

Shanghai Triumphs, Winning All Matches Against Anhui; Result: 3-0

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) In the match between Shanghai and Anhui, Anhui faced Fujian in the preliminary round. Fujian only had two players participating in the doubles match, and they completely forfeited the two singles matches to Anhui, while Fujian's doubles team defeated Anhui. Therefore, Anhui's ability to secure a spot in the second round was purely due to chance, and their strength was only so-so. In the second round, they met Shanghai. Shanghai's talents are average, but the skills of the first singles player, Mao Yuwen, are particularly good. Anhui's Liu Yufang is far from being her opponent, so it formed a one-sided situation. As a result, Mao Yuwen won with two consecutive scores of 6-1.

Shanghai has already won the first singles match. Anhui forfeited the second singles match. Shanghai's Xia Lanzheng defeated Anhui's Sun Silan, with a score of 6-2, 7-5. Therefore, Shanghai won 3-0.

Shanxi Is Fierce, Eliminating Nanjing; Result: 2-1

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) In the match between Shanxi and Beijing, Shanxi's Wang Chunjing's skills are skilled and unusually calm. It is a pity that her shots lack power. The reason for her victory lies entirely in the accuracy of her cross-court shots, making her opponent tired of running and watching her defeat. In the match against Beijing's Liu Yulan on the 15th, Wang also won in this way, with a score of 6-4, 6-1. Wang won two consecutive sets.

(Another Dispatch) The Beijing-Shanxi doubles match started at 2 PM. Shanxi's Sun Guixiu and Chang Shixi's skills were weak and unremarkable. Beijing's Chen Qing and Chen Xibao had good cooperation and average skills, but they were slightly better than Shanxi. Therefore, after two sets, Beijing won with a score of 6-1. The second singles match was the key to the victory or defeat of Beijing and Shanxi. Shanxi had already won a singles match in the morning, so the two sides competed fiercely. Shanxi's Wang Chunwei's skills were skilled, especially her backhand, and she was as calm as her sister Chunjing. Beijing's Huang Shannong's smashes were powerful, and her skills were quite impressive. There was a high possibility of winning this match, but because she was overly cautious, she missed good opportunities, and finally lost two consecutive sets with a score of 7-9, 3-6. Therefore, Shanxi eliminated Beijing with a score of 2-1 and secured a spot in the semifinals.

Sichuan Works Hard and Defeats Hebei; Result: 2-1

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) In the match between Sichuan and Hebei, the situation was more tense. Sichuan's Bao Dajing's smashes were fierce, but Hebei's Cui Shuzhen also resisted fiercely. In the first set, Bao only won with a score of 6-4. In the second set, Bao sailed smoothly, while Cui had difficulty resisting. As a result, Bao won again with a score of 6-1.

(Another Dispatch) The doubles and second singles matches between Sichuan and Hebei were not played because one side forfeited. Sichuan only had two representatives participating, so of course both sides forfeited to Hebei, while Hebei and Beijing only had three players. Since the first singles match had already been played and the doubles match was stipulated by the conference, the second singles match also had to be forfeited to Sichuan. However, Sichuan had already won a singles match in the morning, so Sichuan eliminated Hebei with a score of 2-1 and immediately secured a spot in the semifinals.

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) In the two second-round men's basketball games starting at 9 AM on the 15th, the basketball court was packed with spectators, leaving no room to move. When the first game between Hebei and Fujian started, Fujian made a desperate effort to resist tenaciously, and the situation seemed average. Hebei had smooth sailing, always taking the lead, and the score difference was usually around twenty points. Although Fujian lost, their performance in the second half was commendable. Therefore, Xijue scored a lot of points. In the end, Hebei won 47-29. The referees were Shu Hong and Tong Furan.

Jiangsu Fights Valiantly but Is Defeated Miserably

The Jiangsu team is the essence of a province, with members of Soochow as the backbone, supplemented by athletes from Datong Institute of Physical Education. Until the score was 3-5, the three generals in the front row started to kill, passing the ball to the net and killing it smoothly, which was very clever. The score became 7-7. The color people and others watching the battle on the stand shouted, "Again!" The ball unexpectedly poured into Jiangsu's front court. Guangdong 11, Jiangsu 8 points. Changing sides and fighting again, Jiangsu saw that the incoming ball was hard and fast, and the door was ineffective, the line was scattered and unbearable, and the failure to turn the rollers ended in failure. Guangdong killed Jiangsu with twenty-one to nine, causing fresh blood to flow. In the second game, Jiangsu desperately tried to recover the lost ground, but was impatient and chaotic, with continuous mistakes. Guangdong won eight points in one go. Afterwards, Guangdong's front row committed a net touch foul, and Jiangsu profited from the loophole. The first half was eleven to eight, with Guangdong still having the upper hand. The second half was one-sided, even more dangerous, ending with twenty-one to nine. In the third game, Jiangsu continued to attack tirelessly, jumping back and forth, unwilling to relax a step. The score was close to Guangdong, and the cheers were thunderous. Chen Rushu's serves were effective, and Cui Honghuan's pressure ball was powerful, but unfortunately there were not many opportunities, ending the game with twenty-one to eighteen. The overall result was three to zero, a miserable defeat for Jiangsu. The referee was Li Yunfei.

Guangdong Breaks Record Again in the 400-meter Relay Final—44.4 Seconds—

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) In the 1600-meter relay final, the participants included five teams: Guangdong, Shanghai, Beiping, Hebei, and Nanjing. Although Liaoning had previously won the first group in the preliminary round, Liu Changchun was unable to carry the team alone, so Liaoning forfeited the final. The teams from Beiping, Shanghai and Guangdong started to pull ahead, and then Shanghai and Guangdong went neck and neck. Subsequent Match Results: Hong Kong Meets Strong Opponent, Wins After Hard Fight; Result is 3-1 Win Over Hunan; Hunan's Setting and Coordination are Poor; Beiping Misses Are Truly Powerful, Overcome Jiangsu 3-0

Beiping's Great Victory Over Jiangsu—Three to Zero—Beiping's Generals Certainly Have Real Strength; Jiangsu's Soldiers are Very Soft

In the Beiping women's volleyball preliminary round, they won 3-0, showing that the generals of northern China are indeed extraordinary. This morning, they faced Jiangsu in the subsequent round. Jiangsu is based in Wuxi and includes the iron volleyball generals of Suzhou. However, having had a bye, they had not participated in the preliminary round, so their strength was yet to be seen. From the start of the match, it was clear that they were very soft. They suffered a crushing defeat of 10-21 in the first set. In the second set, Yang Luyi scored a point with a spike, jumping up in the front row for a light kill. This was the most exciting performance from Jiangsu. However, the Beiping misses were ultimately a powerful force that shook northern China, so they did not relax their grip. They won the second set 21-16. In the third set, Jiangsu collapsed completely. Although they brought in reinforcements, their ammunition was exhausted and their generals were tired, so they were ultimately unable to recover. The score was 10-21. Beiping won three straight sets to secure the right to the semi-finals. The referee was Tan Tianpei.

In summary, Hunan's serves were powerful, and their spikes were strong, but their setting and coordination were not as good as the Hong Kong team's. Hong Kong's victory was due to their coordination.

Please pay attention and do not be late.

Predictions for Men's and Women's Swimming Championships

The Dispute Between Guangdong and Hong Kong; The Size of the Swimming Pool

— Oldest

The pool is 50 meters long and 20 meters wide. It is entirely made of mosaic, clean and beautiful. It can accommodate nine people in a race at a time. It is the largest swimming pool in our country. On the two banks of the pool, in addition to the rest area for athletes, there are two square flat diving boards. The open space on both sides is more than ten feet wide. The grandstand is terraced, about two feet wide, half of which is cement and half is green grass, about sixty meters long. Each side has more than ten steps and can accommodate more than a thousand people. At one end of the pool are the changing room, shower room, office, and medicated water pool. Before entering the pool, one must wash their body and feet with medicated water, and their physical fitness must be inspected by the health department, which is extremely strict. It is a pity that there is no warm water shower after swimming, which is a shortcoming.

Diligence in Practice

As the swimming competition date approaches, starting on October 10th, swimmers from provinces and cities participate in timed practice from morning to night. The weather has been cold these days, and the athletes are calling out that it is too cold, but the Shi brothers practice the most diligently, twice a day, each time for more than an hour. They have succeeded because of this.

The Method of This Tennis Competition is Poor; Singles Players Cannot Also Play Doubles; The First and Second Singles Are Not Specified; Since the Start of the Competition, There Have Been Countless Forfeits; If There is Cunning, There is No Way to Handle It

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) The men's and women's tennis competitions are divided into singles and doubles groups. This method is not necessarily bad, but single players should also be allowed to play doubles. This point causes many inconveniences for units that lack talent or are limited by other reasons and cannot send many representatives. Therefore, since the start of the competition, there have been several forfeits every day. However, when the singles are divided one game apiece, the final victory must be determined in doubles. But when both sides have no other doubles players, both sides will inevitably forfeit. How will this group's victory or defeat be resolved? This is an extremely difficult problem, and the organizers did not consider it at the beginning, which has sown the seeds of disaster. It can be said to be extremely brainless. The negligence in handling affairs is even more obvious here. Also, since singles cannot also play doubles, the first and second singles players are not specified. If a player is clearly the first singles player but deliberately changes to the second singles player in order to be cunning, and the official second singles player is promoted to the first singles player, it is deliberately making the victory or defeat of the competition dependent on doubles. But on the one hand, there are no doubles players, and they can only forfeit. Thus, one side will naturally win. Although this is related to sportsmanship and is purely ideal, it is also a very possible event. If such a fact occurs, what will the organizers of the competition do? In short, it cannot be denied that the organizers of this competition lack experience.

Batavia Requests Accommodation

In this National Games tennis championship, eighteen units have participated from across the country and from overseas Chinese. Among them, the Batavia Overseas Chinese Tennis Team is the most eye-catching. Xu Chengji, a member of the team, is the current Java tennis singles champion. At the same time, Lin Xuyin, a member of the team, and Xu teamed up and also won the doubles championship. Their skills must be extraordinary. On the morning of the 12th, the team first met the Hubei team. Xu and Lin both won their singles matches against their opponents 3-0. Unfortunately, in the doubles match held in the afternoon, Xu and Lin were restricted by the committee. Since they had participated in the singles, they could not participate in the doubles, so they were unable to take to the court. The audience was very disappointed, and the players themselves were very dissatisfied. It is said that the team formally sent a written request to the competition committee that afternoon, asking for accommodation. The result is still unknown, but the games were originally held to promote sports and to observe the strengths of the nation's athletes. Therefore, the fair proposal of the Batavia team may not be completely ignored.

The Appeal of Shanghai and Fujian Women's Basketball is Great; Soldiers Vie for Seats

(Nanjing, 15th Dispatch) This morning's women's basketball game between Fujian and Shanghai. The strength of both sides is unusually strong. The audience squeezed into all the gaps. On the southwest grandstand, two students from a certain political school and more than a hundred armed soldiers had a dispute over seats. The soldiers punched each other, and the order was disrupted for a time. The students knew they were at a disadvantage, so they jumped over the railing and fled east. The soldiers chased after them tightly, holding the students down and using whips and wooden sticks to beat them. The students' heads were broken and bleeding, and they shouted for help. The audience was furious and shouted "Catch the bandits!" The guards heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, with bayonets and pistols in hand, surrounding the hundred or so soldiers. Then, they all bowed their heads and listened to orders. The two officers in charge were taken to the headquarters tent near the entrance of the venue. Armed soldiers and police heavily guarded the outside of the tent to prevent accidents. Not long after, the headquarters of the 88th Division called and lightly released the two officers. A storm was quelled.

Athletes Must Train Regularly

The National Games have been held for six days, and Shanghai has won four championships in the men's track and field all-around competition and the women's track and field. This success is due to the concentration of talent and, more importantly, to the effectiveness of regular training. The Shanghai Diligence Bookstore has invited national sports experts to co-author a series of sports books, including: Zhang Heng's (Central University sports instructor) "Track and Field Training Method" (deluxe edition, two yuan); Wang Fudan's (Jiangnan Institute of Physical Education principal) "Track and Field Refereeing Method" (sixty cents); Hao Gengsheng's (Shandong University director of physical education) "Pentathlon and Decathlon Training Method" (ninety-five cents); Hitoimi Kinu’e's "Female Athletes Before the Competition" (ninety cents); Wang Fudan's "Cross-Country Running Training Method" (forty cents); Lu Xiangqian's (Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation chairman) "Race Walking Training Method" (sixty cents). Each book describes the training methods in detail and has many illustrations. They are essential reference books for sports instructors and athletes.

Fire Safety Equipment is Safe at the National Games

The fire safety equipment at the National Games is very careful. In view of the fact that the fire extinguishers manufactured by the family workshops are different in structure from ordinary ones, the anchor pipe is equipped with a belt that can be tilted and fired straight into the flat top inside and the oil pool in the cellar, without leaking gas. The content is a thick-walled glass tube, straight to the bottom, with more capacity than usual. They have written a special letter to borrow fifty units for emergencies, praising their products as being suitable for use. The original letter is as follows: [The fire extinguisher manufactured by your company is well-made and effective, and has long been praised by the Chinese people. The association plans to build temporary sheds this time, mostly for the safety of the venue equipment, and plans to ask your factory to lend 50 fire extinguishers in case of emergencies].

Public Exhibition Cup

YMCA Actively Prepares for International Handball Tournament; Old Court Converted to Standard Style; Member Ranking Competition to be Held

Every year, the Shanghai YMCA organizes the Chinese Handball Team to compete against the Western team of the Western YMCA for the International Handball Public Exhibition Cup. This winter, it will begin again on November 23rd. The association, in light of the Chinese team's previous failures, believes that it was not due to a lack of skill or experience but rather due to differences in the field and rules. Therefore, it has invested heavily to convert the old court into a standard style. At the same time, member ranking competitions will be held on the standard court. In addition to the original ten members, more than twenty people are participating in the preliminary rounds, which is very popular. Everyone who is proficient in this sport is included. After the preliminary rounds, the winners Hua Fenggang, Yan Peiqiu, Cai Tongshou, Xia Zeren, Yuan Zongji, and Yan Zhaorong, along with the aforementioned ten members, will participate in the member ranking competition starting from the 23rd.
