Spring and Autumn

Ma Jie-fu and Judge Lu

— Jun Ti

Ma Jie-fu and Judge Lu, these two names, those who have read "Liaozhai" probably know them. The fact is this...

Ma Jie-fu and Yang Wan-shi were close friends. Wan-shi was naturally afraid of his wife, so afraid that even Ma Jie-fu couldn't stand it, so he gave him a dose of "Husband Rejuvenation Powder," and he indeed overcame his wife. Unfortunately, after the medicine wore off, Wan-shi still lived the life of a kneeling washboard.

Judge Lu and Zhu Er-dan were close friends. Er-dan's writing was too poor, so Judge Lu picked a clever seven-aperture heart in the underworld and replaced it for him, and indeed his writing improved greatly; Er-dan also disliked his wife's unattractive face, so Judge Lu picked an unparalleled face in the mortal world and replaced it for her, and indeed she became alluring.

From this, we can see that Ma Jie-fu's methods are not as good as Judge Lu's: one only teaches him to be excited for a while, and the result is that he is as weak as before; the other is a thorough reform, and the result is that the roots are cut off forever.

We Chinese people are suffering from a disease of weakness, and we happen to meet Ma Jie-fu, who only knows how to give him Rejuvenation Powder, but we have not met Judge Lu to change his heart and reform his face, resulting in a paper tiger that is completely defeated by the opponent.

Moreover, the Rejuvenation Powder we take is more and more than Yang Wan-shi: we took a dose on May 9th, a dose on May 30th, a dose on May 3rd, and recently, we took another dose on September 18th. As we continue to take it, civil officials declare unity; military generals send telegrams requesting battle; merchants claim to resist goods, and students are even more amazing, wearing military uniforms, carrying long guns, and becoming reserve soldiers. It's like Yang Wan-shi cutting off two pieces of meat from his wife with a knife and still not being relieved of his anger. But five minutes later, the effect of the medicine does not rush upwards but leaks downwards, and as a result, Yang Wan-shi still kneels in front of the washboard, and our civil officials, military generals, merchants, and students are still lifeless.

From now on, we must not take Ma Jie-fu's Husband Rejuvenation Powder anymore, but rather ask Judge Lu to change our hearts and reform our faces!

Modern Ghosts

— Drunken Fool

In these times, being a person certainly requires being "modernized." Speaking must be modern, decoration must be modern, and everything from daily life to food and drink must strive for modernity. Only then does one meet the qualifications of a "modern upper-class man and woman, a beautiful person." Otherwise, one is a "corrupt element," an "outdated person of the times." Therefore, in recent years, people have felt a modern craze. The word "modern" was once all the rage. Now it is being extended even further, and even being a ghost requires modernization. If you don't believe it, just look at the advertisement for XX Funeral Home published in the newspaper a few days ago. The content goes like this:

Artistic and magnificent coffins, each sold for洋X千X百X十X元 (a price in foreign currency). Funeral service fees: X百X十元 (another price). Purchasing a coffin alone is also acceptable: this coffin is carved from only two pieces of wood, exquisitely crafted, and modern in style, proving that it will never decay...

Using the title of "modern" on a coffin seems to be a first-time occurrence. One can certainly compose two lines of poetry: "Entering this coffin, one can be a modern ghost." One can also drop a few literary phrases: "Having exhausted beauty and goodness, one can be said to be happy within. There is no one who dies with eyes that will not close." Such modern and new-style coffins are of course for wealthy modern people to enjoy. Although one coffin accompanies the body and everything is over, what's the point of talking about being modern or not? However, Confucius also had the clear instruction of "worship as if they are present," showing future generations. This shows that people and ghosts should be equal: when a person is alive, they like to talk about being modern, and at night they still have to sleep on a modern, new-style bed. After death, they should also sleep in that modern, new-style coffin. Only then can it be considered "consistent from beginning to end, as if still alive even in death."

Speaking of our country's coffins: for thousands of years, they have adhered to old ways and do not know how to improve. Although the wood may be valuable, the form is outdated and without any beauty. The name is a coffin, truly rich in the color of "longevity," making people not want to look at it. Now it's good, coffins also need special improvement and talk about being modernized. I think once this trend starts, others will follow suit, and "modern coffin shops" are bound to spring up one after another. Various new-style coffins will be displayed in categories. Or open a "coffin exhibition" for people to visit. To be even more modern, simply have a "21-day big sale." When that time comes, who knows, the storefront might be like a marketplace, with crowds gathering!

Ramblings on Cartoons

— (Written by Qian Yun, Drawn by Lian Liang)

—Chinese Temperament—

On the street, a small vendor selling socks, because a customer bargained too low, went from showing anger on his face to scolding aloud. The customer, fearing trouble, turned around and quietly avoided him. The further he walked away, the louder the scolding became, probably afraid of not hearing it. Many bystanders giggled.

A Western policeman came along. He didn't have time to carry his bundle away and was grabbed and beaten. This was illegal. He silently endured the beating and then pleaded. Many bystanders giggled.

Finally, he was arrested and taken to the police station. After the dramatic end, the crowd had no more excitement to watch and lazily dispersed.

Initially, no one scolded the vendor for being fierce to the customer, and later no one interceded with the Western policeman. These bystanders simply observed from beginning to end. Giggling and laughing all the time.

Record of Su You Viewing Treasures

Tao Wang is a world-renowned tile of Chai Kiln, handed down through generations by Zhu Zhuping, a reclusive gentleman in Wuzhong, worth a thousand gold. There were few of them even in the Song Dynasty, who would have thought that many remained in the world. I read the gentleman's catalog, with inscriptions by contemporary figures: "The noble recluse is poor and frugal, I am invited to appreciate the treasure leisurely, I move the lamp and stroke it repeatedly, surpassing the view of the setting sun over the river." In my humble view, how can its beauty be exhausted in this alone! Today I am fortunate to feast my eyes, thanks to the introduction of Ms. Zhao Hanying, a renowned expert in epigraphy. Truly, this trip has not been in vain.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Sixteen: Sour Feelings Still Offer Blessings in the Face of the Present, Hurried Military Life Secretly Shifts Troops

The mules and horses in the army camp also have a keen sense of the arrival of war. When the swift wind sweeps across the sky, the loud neighing of the horses has a somewhat frightening undertone. Zhao Ziqiang, upon hearing this sound, felt a kind of indescribable emotion in his heart. He felt even more that his hasty departure, leaving his old father in Haidian, solely to deal with the Yang family mother and daughter, was a matter of his own self-inflicted trouble. He should have discussed it with his father first to put his mind at ease. Now was a good time to take a trip. Although two platoon leaders had left the camp, his limited hours of travel would probably not cause any delays. So he greeted the sergeant and quartermaster, and walked out of the camp. At this time, the sun was setting on the western mountain peak, only a dozen feet high. The boundless wheat field was painted with a golden ray of sunlight. The southeast wind on the plains was no longer so gentle, blowing on people in the setting sun, feeling somewhat chilly. Looking at the small houses in the distance, they seemed to be sinking into the mainland. A person walking on the road, the soles of his shoes making a rustling sound on the lime road. But when a person walks alone, this sound not only does not add to the liveliness but adds a lot of loneliness. Zhao Ziqiang thought, "I plan to walk this road every day after getting married. But that's just wishful thinking. What's the point of being a soldier? One's body belongs to others, and one's life also belongs to others. Perhaps walking this road today will be the last time." Thinking of telling his father these thoughts, guessing how sad he would be; telling Yang Guizhi these thoughts, what would she do? Women's tears are easily... I'm afraid she would faint from crying! No, maybe she would hate me for not shedding a single tear. Alas! When I see them, how can I express these bitter feelings? The more he thought, the slower his pace became, only the wind blowing through the wheat seedlings, rustling, stirring the loneliness in his soul. Suddenly, a burst of bugle sound came from behind. He abruptly stopped. He would not go home. (213)

Regulations for Receiving Payment

The office distributes payments from the 6th to the 10th of each month and again from the 16th to the 20th, except for Sundays, from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM at the accounting department of this office. Please prepare a receipt, affix it with the same seal as the original manuscript, and collect the payment directly. If collecting payments for several months, please prepare separate receipts with seals for each month for attachment to the ledger. Regarding the sealing, regardless of the length of the article or the number of submissions per month, please affix a seal to each article for verification of the seal upon collection. If no seal is affixed, the payment will be rejected. Furthermore, the payment period is six months from the date of publication. If the payment remains uncollected by the deadline, it will be considered as not accepted, and the account will be canceled to close the matter. Shen Bao Chunqiu Editorial Department

General Mobilization of Laughter

— Mei Xue

Pots of the same origin do not sympathize with each other, but those of the same kind injure each other

Once, at the launching ceremony of a warship, Mrs. So-and-so, the wife of a certain minister, was invited to perform the bottle-breaking ceremony. This lady had received an education and was always ashamed of showing off. Breaking a champagne bottle in front of the public was not mentioned in the Biographies of Exemplary Women or Rules for Women's Chambers, so of course, she was ashamed of showing off. Since the lady refused to participate in the bottle-breaking ceremony, the minister had no choice but to send a female employee to represent the lady in performing the bottle-breaking ceremony. This female employee was a delicate red flower vase. She was very happy to accept this modern mission and participate. When she returned after breaking the bottle, a male employee who often told jokes said to her with a smile, "The red flower vase breaks the champagne bottle, it is not sympathizing with pots of the same origin, but injuring those of the same kind." Those who heard it laughed loudly, and the red flower vase's face turned red, all the way to her ears.

The exploited calligrapher and painter

Once a calligrapher and painter becomes famous, many relatives and old friends try to exploit them, either paying half the price or nothing at all. Occasional exploitation is understandable, but the most hateful thing is doing it again and again, endlessly, making it difficult for the calligrapher and painter to comply. Calligraphers and painters call this kind of exploitation "overstepping." If they keep overstepping, the painter often inscribes a couplet for them, embedding the poetic phrase "transcending the image." When the painter paints for them, he often draws a large water pot, with a glimpse of a dipper handle protruding from the water pot. These are all meant to be "singing to the zither," hoping that they will not overstep again after this overstepping. It is said that someone asked someone to paint an ancient beauty, specifying ten dollars, but when it came to paying the advance fee, he only wanted to pay five dollars. The painter insisted on painting a concubine Xu showing half her face. The man was displeased and said, "There are many ancient beauties, why only paint this concubine Xu with half her face made up?" The painter smiled and said, "The fee you paid is also a half-face makeup." Also, someone asked someone to paint a fan without paying a penny. The second time he asked that person to paint a fan again. That person wrote a Tang poem, omitting four words. It wrote: "Last year today, in this door, peach blossoms reflected each other in red: I don't know where to go? Peach blossoms still smile in the spring breeze." The man said, "Sir, you're wrong. The second line omits the words 'human face', and the third line also omits the words 'human face'." The calligrapher smiled and said, "So you still want a face? I thought you didn't want a face either time, so I omitted two human faces for you."

The Nude Movement of Peanuts

Recently, the nude movement has not been accomplished. Not to mention that people have a sense of shame, even the peanuts without a sense of shame, after being stripped of a coat, still have a tight-fitting red shirt. They are unwilling to strip completely. There is also a kind of white peanut that is stripped completely naked: but it is easy to get damp, easy to reduce the fragrance, and not as palatable as the peanut with a shirt on. Therefore, the nude movement of peanuts is largely in a state of failure. Now that August has arrived, sugar-roasted chestnuts are on the market. The chestnuts from Liangxiang are very open-minded girls, with a light twist, the outer shirt and underwear are all stripped clean. I ate a local chestnut the other day, stripped of its outer shirt. Don't think you can strip off its underwear. Later, I hardened my wrists and reluctantly stripped it off, pinching off a layer of the chestnut's flesh. I said: This chestnut refuses to strip off its underwear, willing to have its skin shattered, it has the attitude of a chaste woman in ancient times, I am disrespectful.

A Bird's-Eye View of Medicine in Shanghai in the Last Decade (Continued)

— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter Six: Medical Education and Publications

(20) Medical Monthly Singapore Chinese Medicine Association

In addition, omissions are unavoidable. I have less interest in this kind of publication, so the investigation may not be as thorough, and various quarterly graduation publications of Chinese medicine schools are also not included.

Except for the first item, National Medicine Review, which is a special awakening of the youth, a new public opinion of national medicine, all the other nineteen kinds of old medical publications were produced to oppose the new medicine. Because these publications were almost all published after 1928. That year, at the Central Health Conference, someone proposed to limit the production of old medicine, so publications sprung up for a time, making resistance propaganda. In places with more new medicine, they also had more publications. As for the writers, most of them were those who claimed to be communication factions and Chinese medicine school factions. (Making resistance) It seems that after reading a few superficial books on physiology and hygiene, and some pharmaceutical factory brochures, they saw all the new medicine at a glance, immediately launched a general attack, eloquent and arrogant, but in reality, full of fallacies. On one hand, they were considered wild fox Zen by the conservative faction of old medicine, and on the other hand, they were not pleasing to anyone. Therefore, some of them often rose and fell quickly, and finally stopped publishing. Some were edited by more conservative people, mostly publishing proven prescriptions and ancient cases, making business calls, clearly shouting that medicine cannot be abolished, for the livelihood of the old medicine community. This was also straightforward and honest. The most wonderful group of merchants simply used publishing to advertise and solicit business, with the tone of "While I am lucky for ten years, come and see a doctor early." When their career was thriving, they also stopped writing. If you ask what kind of "scientific" articles and "communication faction" communication methods were published in these publications, I am limited in space here, and my bird's-eye view has ended with the five chapters of the main text. Now, let me just extract some famous quotes below as their representatives, so that readers can hold their stomachs after the depression, which is my final speech.

China's establishment is on the back of the earth (see Medical Spring and Autumn)

Gypsum must be used raw {its sulfur nourishment is light, its properties are cool and can disperse {if calcined, the sulfur nourishment will fly away, and the remaining calcium after calcination will become cement {if accidentally ingested, it can solidify a person's blood vessels (see Medical Spring and Autumn)

Radix Bupleuri reduces fever and loosens lymphatic vessels (see One Remark on the Medical Forest)

For decades, I have never heard of a Western doctor who can connect bones and tendons (ibid.)

It is advisable to imitate the meaning of the scrofula-dispersing powder in the Golden Mirror to eliminate scrofula and kill bacteria (Common Sense of Family Medicine, Mr. Wang Shenxuan's wonderful explanation of tuberculosis)

When using aconite and dried ginger to excite their nerves (Common Sense of Family Medicine)

Meningitis bacteria have not yet been discovered (see Health Report)

Cholera is caused by dampness stagnation with middle cold (Meixian Medical Monthly)

Collaterals are micro-capillaries that carry qi and blood, communicating internally with the stomach and externally with the muscles (Jilin Medical Monthly)

Postpartum mammary gland secretion is due to the sympathetic nerve inhibition and autonomic nerve promotion, hence women take Yinqiao as the meridian (Shanxi Medical Journal)

Earth is equal to chemical force, which is gravity, also known as neutralizing force. Phase fire is electric heat, that is, electric current (Shanxi Medical Journal)

Seafood and dried meat have no place for bacteria to stay {injecting salt water and rubbing salt all over the bodies of Mongolian people have the same meaning (Xiashi Medical Report)

The maxillary artery, nasal artery, and preauricular artery are divided into heaven, earth, and man (Singapore Medical Monthly)

The Ling Shu's so-called "passing through the genitals to reach the lower abdomen" is actually the capillary of the umbilical vein (Medical Spring and Autumn)

Qi transformation is the mother of cells, and the six excesses are the mother of bacteria (Wuxian Medical Report)

In addition, Xingfu Bao widely introduces single prescriptions, Shijie Yibao talks a lot about plague test recipes, and regardless of whether there is isolation, Yunti Qiao's various bacterial theories are colorful and very interesting.

Discussions on Jiao Yitang's Letter to the Nation Regarding the Adoption of National Medicine Regulations (Continued)

— Yu Yunxiu

Using silk and tea as an analogy, the Chinese medicine industry's rice bowl is shrinking and breaking day by day. It can be predicted that it will inevitably decline. At the same time, the number of people who rely on the medicine industry for a living is increasing. However, besides using scientific methods to revitalize the silk and tea industries and the methods I have proposed to save the declining industry, what other way out is there? My rescue methods were published on the first page, number 84, of the Social Medical Gazette, which was the special issue on domestic drugs published on February 16th of this year. The article [The Fundamental Work of China's Drug Problem] advocated four measures: first, replacing foreign drugs; second, manufacturing raw materials; third, conducting scientific research on Chinese drugs; and fourth, observing and verifying Chinese drugs. If we diligently advance along the scientific path, why should we fear increasing costs and unemployment? Alas, Mr. Jiao! As long as you have a clear goal and work hard towards it, you don't have to worry about not having proper solutions. You can always remedy losses and prevent malpractices. Why insist on reversing course and taking a dead end?

Therefore, in my opinion, whether from an academic perspective, a doctor allocation perspective, or a national economic perspective, abolishing national medicine clearly has great benefits and no drawbacks.

Mr. Jiao said: [The empiricism of national medicine constantly presents facts to people, which clearly has its material basis. As long as we use scientific methods to explain it, it will naturally become a systematic discipline.] According to what I said above, the empiricism signboard of national medicine is a false new title. The facts presented, when explored from a theoretical perspective, cannot escape the realm of "lucky coincidence." National medicine, which lacks material civilization progress, naturally has no material basis. Explaining it using scientific methods is like an old village woman wearing high heels, becoming a world monster, and is not worth talking about as an academic discipline.

Mr. Jiao, science certainly needs a system, but having a system does not necessarily mean it can masquerade as science. The old astrology, medicine, divination, and the theories of the Five Elements have been passed down through generations, with everyone singing the same tune. We cannot say it has no system, but it lacks a scientific basis. Therefore, in modern times, it cannot be considered an academic discipline. Your entire national medicine is already irreparably broken and has declared its demise in the midst of calls for [organizing it in a scientific way]. Even Mr. Jiao cannot but admit that a part of metaphysics should be abandoned. But whether the remaining scales and claws after the shattering and demise can be accommodated in the scientific world depends on the results of future research by scientists. If the results are good, they can certainly survive; if the results are not good, they will certainly perish together. The fate of national medicine is just like this, and what can be hoped for is only this. The only way we can promote national glory is to do this. Therefore, those who want to do their part for national medicine can only encourage scientists to research it. This is the only way out for the remaining scales and claws after the shattering and demise. Without starting with research, and superficially using a bit of scientific knowledge to interpret things in a far-fetched way, no matter how systematic it becomes, it will be useless. Mr. Jiao's proposal is completely for the problem of your national medicine practitioners, setting a short-sighted and delaying tactic; it is not for the issue of academics, planning for a permanent existence, or far-sighted planning.

Mr. Jiao said: [It is unbearable that the government does not pay deep attention to it, and would rather allow Western countries to establish Chinese medicine lectures and promote research. In the domestic education system, there is no place for national medicine.] Mr. Jiao, you need to understand! It's not that national medicine has no place in the education system, it's that metaphysics has no place in the education system. Outside of world medical science, there is absolutely no possibility for the existence of national medicine, so of course it has no place. There are now several private national medicine schools. Please, Mr. Jiao, take out their lecture notes and announce whether they are suitable for modern education or not. The reason why national medicine cures diseases is, of course, inexplicable. Taking a step back, even if you know the reason, according to Mr. Jiao's words, you cannot tell others. Then, standing on the podium, you can only look at the students. How can you educate the youth? Mr. Jiao! Western countries establish Chinese medicine lectures in the hands of scientific physicians, to digest Chinese medicine into scientific medicine, as a branch of scientific medicine. Your national medicine schools advocate putting the power of scientific organization in the hands of metaphysicians, to attach science to the surface of metaphysics, and to be independent outside of scientific medicine. Western countries only allow scholars who have completed scientific medical training to become graduate students, and the instructors are even above them. Your national medicine schools advocate having national medicine practitioners with no scientific literacy decorate the scientific facade, and the leaders are even below them. Western countries do not establish separate Chinese medicine schools outside of medical schools, nor do they have Chinese medicine figures outside of physicians. Your national medicine schools advocate opening up a separate position in the education system, and having Chinese medicine figures outside of scientific medicine. Western countries are completely about theoretical research. Your national medicine schools are completely about business exclusion. The goals, behaviors, strategies, and backgrounds are completely different. It's embarrassing that you, sir, brought them up as an analogy.

Mr. Jiao said: Repeatedly in terms of business, national medicine's treatment of diseases cannot but be said to belong to hygiene, but the hygiene administrative organs have no officials in charge of national medicine. When problems arise, they arbitrarily teach personnel who do not understand national medicine to solve them. For example, two or three months ago, the Shanghai National Medicine Association and the Shanghai National Medicine Branch had a dispute and appealed to the Executive Yuan, which planned to transfer it to the Ministry of Health for review. Medical science is indeed a matter of hygiene, but the Chinese Ministry of Health does not recognize national medicine at all, so how can it review it? When the Legislative Yuan passed the Western Medicine Regulations, the health authorities declared that they would soon propose national medicine regulations, but the regulations have not been drafted for a long time. The central government, recognizing the urgency of managing national medicine, first established the Central National Medicine Hall in the 20th year of the Republic [1931]. Subsequently, in June of this year, it drafted national medicine regulations. Xiang Fei

For example, the Central Political Conference has strictly prohibited the premature

announcement of cases that have not been passed. I don't know what means the Tianjin Dagongbao Medical Supplement used to publish the draft in advance and distort it, saying that the establishment of the National Medicine Hall undermines the health administration system. The National Medicine Hall's undermining of the health administration system is indeed as said, but it is not known that China's health administration system is not perfect. If Mr. Jiao believes that there are capable people in the Western medical community, then as long as your national medicine practitioners have the courage and ability to take on this lecture, I will definitely take on the responsibility of petitioning and requesting them to establish national medicine lectures to employ your national medicine practitioners as professors. But you must not walk into the laboratory, see the microscope, test tube, and various excellent instruments, be stunned and speechless, and make a joke. The shortcoming of the Ministry of Health is only that the national medicine regulations have not been drafted for a long time and that there are no responsible officials. Regarding this, our Chinese Medical Association has already submitted a memorial to the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Central Political Conference, urging them to draft these regulations as soon as possible. At that time, responsible officials will naturally appear. Those who want to be officials may as well recommend one or two people to go in and take a seat, and they can naturally review the problems that arise in national medicine. I think there is a very correct path to take. Why establish another institution to destroy the administrative system? It's really incomprehensible.

In this wonderful passage of Mr. Jiao, suddenly it is unbearable that the government does not pay deep attention, and suddenly the central government is very urgently managing national medicine. May I ask, is the central government the government? Is the government the central government? It seems that the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Health belong to the government but not to the central government, and the National Medicine Hall belongs to the central government but not to the government, revealing the weakness that policies come from multiple sources and things have no direction. No wonder people laugh at it as an unorganized country. It seems that Mr. Jiao, who is the chairman of the Legislative Yuan's Legal System Committee, should not say such a thing!

Also, the word "Western medicine" is extremely inappropriate. Scientific medicine has now become a global, universally accepted discipline. Where are there east, west, north, and south to distinguish? If we trace its origin, why is the solar calendar that we follow today not called the Western calendar, but instead called the National calendar? Why are the armies carrying guns, cannons, airplanes, and warships not called Western armies? The postal service completely imitates the West. Why not call it Western Post? Why not invite the old-fashioned private postal bureaus of the people to come out and call them National Post? The legal system has completely become Western-style. Why not call it Western Law? Why not invite the old gentlemen of criminal law and money shells to come out and call them National Law? Why not call mathematics, physics, chemistry, etc. in education by their old names from the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, and call them Western Learning? Why is the old name from the Guangxu period being restored only for the term "Western medicine"? To be honest with the people, the original name of the Western Medicine Regulations of the Ministry of Health was Physician Regulations. When it reached the Legislative Yuan, the word "physician" was suddenly changed to the extremely nonsensical "Western medicine." This is because there were a group of narrow-minded national medicine practitioners working as officials in the Legislative Yuan, who made such a joke. They had already occupied a place for national medicine outside of scientific medicine, at least to a limited extent, venting their depression and pleasing their hearts in this name, regardless of whether it was sensible or not, and making the most of the power they wielded today. Alas, Mr. Jiao! Learning requires real ability and strength. Relying on false propaganda and cunning deception, even if you deceive the eyes and ears for a while and gain a day's victory, it is only the setting sun reflecting its light. The future only has the word "extinction" waiting for you. Adding a hundred "national" characters is useless. The strength of science is expanding day by day. Adding a hundred "Western" characters cannot suppress it. Zhuangzi said it well, [The name is the guest of the reality. Shall I be a guest?]

Furthermore, I also have an mimeographed copy of the National Medicine Regulations, and the person who gave it to me said that it was obtained from the branch, and it was easy to get. The Dagongbao probably didn't get it by any means! I have discussed it to this point. Looking at Mr. Jiao's original text, there are only two hundred or so words left, and it is becoming more and more irrational. They can all be easily solved by following the discussions above. I will stop writing here. …(End)

A Sincere Advice to Those Aspiring to Reform Chinese Medicine

— Zhou Sha

After I discussed old medical education, mentioning [A high-achieving student from a Chinese medicine school wrote a letter to Mr. Yu Yunxiu, expressing admiration and taking him as a teacher], Mr. Zhou Sha sent me a letter, stating that he was the one who wrote to Mr. Yu and that he agreed with my arguments, believing that they keenly saw the evils of the old medical community. He also attached a manuscript and asked me to reprint it. The writing is clear, and the views are outstanding. It is admirable. The original text was published in the fourth issue of the National Medicine Review. The authors of that book are mostly fresh and insightful like Mr. Zhou. But those who have received education in Chinese medicine schools, my country's old medicine, originally relied on mysterious and general theories, and were attached to the Confucian education of respecting antiquity to serve the world. Now, new middle school students enter speculative Chinese medicine schools. Let alone the far-fetched and illogical nature of their theories, which is rejected by young people who have received mathematics, physics, and chemistry education, even their training in studying the ancients will inevitably conflict with the reading methods that have been influenced by new literature. It is no different than leading a clever child into the backstage of a magician and forcing them to perform alchemy for the public. Is that possible? National Medicine Review is a sketch and review of the backstage of old medicine. Haha. The younger generation is to be feared. Gentlemen, rest. Pang Jingzhou

The Chinese medical industry is a mixture of old and new, with right and wrong indistinguishable, and absurd and bizarre phenomena can be heard almost everywhere. Although it is due to the lack of unified medical administration, the immaturity of public intelligence is also a major reason. Thus, the so-called problem of reforming Chinese medicine arises, and the proponents of this problem can be roughly divided into two factions. The former is restorationist, and the latter is completely reformist. The former faction mostly consists of non-scientists who claim to be the intellectual class, believing that the history of Chinese medicine is thousands of years old, and there must be values that cannot be erased. Therefore, they vigorously advocate preservation and have the so-called slogan of [scientizing old medicine]. In fact, this faction is full of muddled metaphysicians. Non-scientists do not understand the general trend of world evolution and the degree of scientific development, so they publish these seemingly plausible remarks. It is really a mistake. The latter faction mostly consists of scientists, scholars with clear minds who are not bewitched by metaphysics. Mr. Yu Yunxiu can be taken as a representative of this faction. Mr. Yu has a full understanding of the doctrines of old medicine, and his criticisms of old medicine are completely based on science, seeking truth from facts, with not a single word being a castle in the air. However, his remarks are inevitably too激昂 because he wants to awaken those ignorant and undiscriminating people, (but it was also given to Mr. Yu by the old doctors. The author absolutely does not agree.) and aroused the backlash of the old doctors, even saying that Mr. Yu is fighting for the rice bowl. The absurdity of this kind of argument, clear-headed people can of course see at a glance that it is useless language based on no academic theory and can be ignored. However, one dog barks at a shadow, and a hundred dogs bark in response, which can greatly hinder the bright future of China's medical industry and cannot but be debated. Because as long as non-scientific old medicine and old drugs exist for one day, there will be one more obstacle to China's entire medical industry. Therefore, for the sake of the health of our Chinese nation and for the future of the entire Chinese medical industry, we must do our best to criticize the remarks that maintain absurd and bizarre old medicine. If anyone thinks that advocating scientific medicine is selling the country: advocating old medicine is preserving national essence, then this person's brain has been poisoned to a very deep degree. Since these people are so muddled, why should we still earnestly advise them? Because they and we are both members of the Chinese people, we have to speak loudly to open their confusion. Although it may not be a good thing to improve many domestic products, it is impossible for these muddled scholars who advocate improving Chinese medicine to rely solely on the knowledge gained from a few books to improve it. We can boldly say that the result is [equal to zero]. Without using science as a tool to improve it, no matter how great your abilities are, it will not help in practice. The author does not dare to rashly agree with the so-called scientific old medical reformers. Because I feel that their remarks are not enough to accomplish anything, but more than enough to spoil things: they are drugs that paralyze young people's thoughts. Therefore, I do not overestimate myself and offer some opinions to those who aspire to reform Chinese medicine, and hope to be corrected!

Regarding the entire Chinese medical industry. In this deformed China, it should be discussed from the new and old aspects: The most obvious aspect of the new is the lack of talent; the harm of lack of talent is that the new power (the power of scientific medicine) cannot develop. The old forces are prone to grow, and this is mutually causal. Because the new forces cannot develop; therefore, the old forces are prone to grow. Because the old forces grow more easily, the new forces can only develop less. This situation is not fabricated by the author facing the wall. Anyone who pays a little attention to the state of Chinese medicine can probably know it? (Please refer to Pang Jingzhou's article Shanghai Medical Panorama in the Last Ten Years, published in Shenbao Medical Weekly) In the new aspect, as long as we have the determination and strength, we can always reach the realm of our ideals. However, the old aspect is not the case. A slight negligence in the argument can easily lead astray, making countless promising young people wander and hesitate without knowing where to go. Because of this reason, the so-called problem of reforming old medicine is necessary for us to review.

We will not do the so-called work of improving old medicine, but if we want to do this work, then at the very least we must have the following six conditions. Otherwise, it will naturally waste a lot of valuable brain cells without receiving the slightest effect. Not only is there no effect, but there is also the possibility of hindering the development of [the entire Chinese medical industry]!

(I) Stance

If someone asks me: [Where should we stand to study the good and bad of old medicine, in other words, what attitude should we use to study its good and bad? [Then I must answer him like this: [We should stand on the scientific stance and use scientific means to study the good and bad of old medicine. ] We must know that not standing on the scientific stance to study old medicine will produce various mistakes. Such as the so-called [improving national medicine] by old doctors, he fundamentally divides medicine into geographical boundaries, so if someone says that old medicine should be abolished, he will angrily scold you [patriotic, not knowing how to use it. China has many domestic drugs and many doctors and pharmacies that rely on domestic drugs to make a living. How can he maintain his livelihood? Mr. Tan Cizhong sometimes cannot help but publish such remarks, I weep for the future of China. ] and other laughable words. This is what happens when the stance is wrong. Otherwise, they would never say such short-sighted words. If we stand on the scientific stance, it is not the case. This thing is in accordance with science and beneficial to modern times, then it is allowed to exist. Otherwise, it is restorationist, not in accordance with science, no matter whether it is the law of [ancient and modern China and foreign countries], we must kick it down and do not let it leave a little bit of residue in the world. In short, live if it is in accordance with science, die if it is not in accordance with science, if those who publish non-scientific and restorationist remarks: whether it is our stern father. Or close friends, respected teachers, we must criticize it and overthrow it according to science, the so-called [I love my teacher, I also love the truth. ] is. Comrades! Don't forget this sentence! Because in the scientific universe there is only truth and falsehood, not good and evil, and moreover, doing scholarship is incumbent, isn't it? Remember!

The General State of Latent Tuberculosis and Its Benefits to the Human Body (I)

— Xie Yunshu

The general public often over-fears pulmonary tuberculosis, thus causing the so-called phthisiophobia. However, in recent years, based on autopsies and [tuberculin] reaction calculations, more than 90% of people have pulmonary tuberculosis. Of these 90%, only

The average is latent tuberculosis. For the people of the country who do not yet understand the pathology and recuperation of tuberculosis, I am now the general state of latent tuberculosis and its benefits to the human body. From the lower collection of my translation of the lung disease recuperation teaching rules, I will first extract a paragraph for the public to view.

The General State of Latent Tuberculosis

The state of latent tuberculosis. The author intends to describe it in a little more detail in this section. The meaning of so-called latent tuberculosis is threefold. Readers should be able to understand it after reading it.

(1) Once infected with tuberculosis, it is fully treated due to treatment and health maintenance. The tuberculous lesions in the lungs are surrounded by the increase of connective tissue to form hard knots. However, a few viable tuberculosis bacteria still remain in the center. (The resistance of tuberculosis bacteria is extremely strong, as described in Section 19 of the upper collection.) However, it is difficult to know how long these tuberculosis bacteria will survive from external examination. Although many years have passed, if the body's defense force is greatly reduced, the disease will inevitably recur. This is the so-called recurrence of lung disease. There are no symptoms, and the body is obese, thinking that it is fully treated and very relieved. Because of not maintaining health, the body unknowingly becomes thinner. Fever gradually occurs. The previous lung disease gradually recurs. Or it is caused by sudden hemoptysis. Or lung disease recurs due to other serious illnesses. This is because the health maintenance during the lung disease era was good, but the health maintenance after the recovery period was insufficient. It is really regrettable. Therefore, from the perspective of a doctor, strictly speaking, those who have suffered from pulmonary tuberculosis once cannot be said to be fully treated for a long time in their lives. There are also those who have fully recovered because all tuberculosis bacteria have died, but it is difficult to guarantee that each person is like this. In other words, patients after the recovery period are actually a kind of so-called [latent tuberculosis] throughout their lives. From this point of view, the health maintenance method after the recovery period is really important.

(2) Although the period of formal pulmonary tuberculosis has not been experienced, I do not know how tuberculosis is infected. Tuberculosis bacteria are latent in a certain part of the body. Various symptoms occur that are slightly different from true lung disease. Often, one does not feel that one has tuberculosis at all. This is the so-called true latent tuberculosis. Most of those with weak bodies in childhood and adolescence belong to this state. Later, most of them become true pulmonary tuberculosis. It is difficult for ordinary doctors to diagnose this with general diagnostic methods. If you look at it with the eyes of a specialist, you can understand it at a glance. The so-called lung disease candidates or teenagers with lung disease are mostly in this category. It can be known by the [tuberculin] skin reaction test showing a clear reaction. Now, let's briefly talk about the symptoms that are easily known from the outside. Such as thin body. Although taking a lot of nourishment does not make the surface fat. Pale complexion. No energy. Often easily tired due to trivial matters. And easily suffer from palpitations and hyperactivity. Easily suffer from colds. After suffering from a cold. Difficult to cure after a long time. Easily get fever and cough. Sometimes night sweats. Easily get chest pain and a feeling of pressure in the chest. The stomach and intestines are weak and the appetite is lacking. In women, it is often accompanied by amenorrhea or dysmenorrhea. This is in the world or a part of the doctors. For this kind of latent tuberculosis patients. Most people commonly regard them as anemia, neurasthenia, gastrointestinal disease, gynecological disease. Although considerable treatment can be applied. But it does not take effect for a long time. Because anemia, neurasthenia, gastrointestinal disease, and gynecological disease are only its appearance. And the root is actually latent tuberculosis. If you do not apply the treatment for latent tuberculosis, it is only natural that it cannot be fully cured. (To be continued)
